# Omega

[View source](/wiki/Omega?action=edit) 

* [History](/wiki/Omega?action=history)
* [Purge](/wiki/Omega?action=purge)
* [Talk (43)](/wiki/Talk:Omega)

[![This article details a subject that is considered canon.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](/wiki/Canon "This article details a subject that is considered canon.")[![This page is semi-protected.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](/wiki/Wookieepedia:Protection_policy#Semi-protection "This page is semi-protected.")

[![OnACanonArticle](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](/wiki/Canon "Canon")

For other uses, see **[Omega](/wiki/Omega_(disambiguation) "Omega (disambiguation)")**.

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [Bobawhere](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/Bobawhere.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120228043322) | Boba Fett? Boba Fett? Where? Once finished, remove this notice. | |  |

* Adult
* c. 18 BBY

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Character)

:   "*I would not discount Omega's insight. A state of heightened awareness is not unusual for an enhanced clone such as herself.*"
:   ―Tech, in regards to Omega[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1)

**Omega** was an enhanced [human](/wiki/Human "Human") [female](/wiki/Gender "Gender") [clone](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") created from the [genetic template](/wiki/Clone_template "Clone template") of the [Mandalorian](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian") [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett") who lived in the [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") following the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"). Originally created as a pure genetic replication of Fett, she was a medical assistant to [Kaminoan](/wiki/Kaminoan "Kaminoan") [Chief Medical Scientist](/wiki/Chief_Medical_Scientist "Chief Medical Scientist") [Nala Se](/wiki/Nala_Se "Nala Se") and spent her [days](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day") working in [Tipoca City](/wiki/Tipoca_City "Tipoca City") on the clone [homeworld](/wiki/Planet "Planet") of [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino"). Omega witnessed many clones, including [Hunter](/wiki/Hunter "Hunter"), [Wrecker](/wiki/Wrecker "Wrecker"), [Tech](/wiki/Tech "Tech"), [Echo](/wiki/Echo "Echo"), and [Crosshair](/wiki/Crosshair "Crosshair") of [Clone Force 99](/wiki/Clone_Force_99 "Clone Force 99"), a [squad](/wiki/Squad "Squad") of [clone commandos](/wiki/Clone_commando "Clone commando") with genetic mutations that were also known as the Bad Batch. When the war ended in [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"), Clone Force 99 returned to Kamino from a [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Kaller "Battle of Kaller") on the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Kaller](/wiki/Kaller "Kaller") in the aftermath of [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66") and encountered the newly-created [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"). Omega recognized the squad and was determined to befriend them. Later, when [Admiral](/wiki/Admiral "Admiral") [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin") arrived on Kamino to assess the [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper"), Clone Force 99 rejected the Empire's new orders. Omega would join Clone Force 99 and escape Kamino, although Crosshair chose to stay behind and serve the new regime.

Omega accompanied Clone Force 99 on their subsequent visit to the clone deserter [Cut Lawquane](/wiki/Cut_Lawquane "Cut Lawquane") at his family's [farm](/wiki/Lawquane%27s_Farm "Lawquane's Farm") on the planet [Saleucami](/wiki/Saleucami "Saleucami"), which was her first time away from Kamino. There, she made friends with the Lawquane children, [Shaeeah](/wiki/Shaeeah_Lawquane "Shaeeah Lawquane") and [Jek](/wiki/Jek_Lawquane "Jek Lawquane"), and helped secure the family's escape by delivering forged [chain codes](/wiki/Chain_code "Chain code") to them so they could board a [transport](/wiki/Transport "Transport") offworld. Although Hunter wanted her to go along with the family on the [ship](/wiki/Starship "Starship"), wanting to Omega to grow up with a family instead of being looked after by a group of [soldiers](/wiki/Soldier "Soldier"), Omega insisted on remaining with Clone Force 99.

After Omega drew the attention of the [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [Fennec Shand](/wiki/Fennec_Shand "Fennec Shand") during the Bad Batch's [supply run](/wiki/Chase_on_Pantora "Chase on Pantora") on the [moon](/wiki/Moon "Moon") [Pantora](/wiki/Pantora "Pantora"), the group made their way to the planet [Ord Mantell](/wiki/Ord_Mantell "Ord Mantell") to locate the [informant](/wiki/Information_broker "Information broker") named [Ciddarin Scaleback](/wiki/Ciddarin_Scaleback "Ciddarin Scaleback"), a former associate of the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") during the war. The Bad Batch would begin working for Cid, first completing a [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Ord_Mantell_(Clone_Force_99) "Mission to Ord Mantell (Clone Force 99)") on [Ord Mantell](/wiki/Ord_Mantell "Ord Mantell") in exchange for information on Shand as well as [credits](/wiki/Galactic_Credit_Standard "Galactic Credit Standard") before pulling a [job](/wiki/Mission_to_a_droid_decommissioning_facility "Mission to a droid decommissioning facility") on the planet [Corellia](/wiki/Corellia "Corellia"). Shortly after the latter mission, Omega met [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Rex](/wiki/Rex "Rex"), a former soldier in the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic") and associate of the Bad Batch. When Rex realized that the group still had their [inhibitor chips](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip"), he implored them to get them removed. Omega and the others would join him on the planet [Bracca](/wiki/Bracca "Bracca") so the rest of the group could undergo a procedure inside a downed [*Venator*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Venator-class_Star_Destroyer "Venator-class Star Destroyer") and get the chips removed. After Rex departed, the Batch was discovered by the Empire. After being pursued by Crosshair and his [forces](/wiki/Elite_Squad "Elite Squad"), Omega was eventually kidnapped by a third party: the bounty hunter [Cad Bane](/wiki/Cad_Bane "Cad Bane"). She would eventually escape Bane when he landed at a [cloning facility](/wiki/Bora_Vio_cloning_facility "Bora Vio cloning facility") on the planet [Bora Vio](/wiki/Bora_Vio "Bora Vio") to collect his payment, and after evading Bane and the recently arrived Shand, she was rescued by the other members of the Bad Batch.

When Hunter was captured by the Empire on a [mission](/wiki/Extraction_on_Daro "Extraction on Daro") on the planet [Daro](/wiki/Daro "Daro"), Omega and the others returned to Kamino to rescue him. Omega assisted in freeing him from Crosshair and his squad, but when the Batch tried to flee, [Imperial Star Destroyers](/wiki/Venator-class_Star_Destroyer "Venator-class Star Destroyer") [bombarded](/wiki/Attack_on_Kamino "Attack on Kamino") Tipoca City, completely destroying it. The group, along with the [medical droid](/wiki/Medical_droid "Medical droid") [AZI-3](/wiki/AZI-345211896246498721347 "AZI-345211896246498721347") and Crosshair, followed Omega through the [Kamino tube system](/wiki/Kamino_tube_system "Kamino tube system") back to their [ship](/wiki/Marauder_(Omicron-class) "Marauder (Omicron-class)"), but when the elevator back to the [secret landing platform](/wiki/Secret_landing_platform "Secret landing platform") was damaged, the group floated to the surface in cloning pods, guided through the debris by AZI-3. When the [droid](/wiki/Droid "Droid") sacrificed the last of his power to save Omega, she dived into the [water](/wiki/Water "Water") after him and nearly drowned before being saved by Crosshair. When the Batch offered Crosshair the chance to rejoin them and leave the Empire behind, he declined. Omega thanked him for saving her and reminded him that no matter what, he was still their brother as well as hers before leaving Kamino with her squad.

Omega would go on to become a skilled user of the [Zygerrian energy bow](/wiki/Zygerrian_energy_bow "Zygerrian energy bow") and would accompany the Bad Batch on many jobs and adventures, including on the planets [Serenno](/wiki/Serenno "Serenno"), [Serolonis](/wiki/Serolonis "Serolonis"), [Skara Nal](/wiki/Skara_Nal "Skara Nal"), and [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk"). She and the squad would visit the planet [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant") when Rex asked them to help [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") [Riyo Chuchi](/wiki/Riyo_Chuchi "Riyo Chuchi"), who was fighting for the rights of all clone troopers in the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate"). With their help, Chuchi was able to expose the destruction of Tipoca City as an Imperial deed, but it only amounted to [the Emperor](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") manipulating the Senate into allowing for new military measures that did not benefit the clones. Furthermore, Echo departed from the squad, joining Rex's [Clone Underground](/wiki/Clone_Underground "Clone Underground"). Omega tearfully said goodbye to Echo, although he promised he would not be gone forever. Omega struggled with Echo's absence, and when the *Marauder* was hijacked and stolen on the planet [Ipsidon](/wiki/Ipsidon "Ipsidon"), the squad's tight-knit togetherness was further threatened. Omega grew frustrated with her brothers and their willingness to move on and accept change, although after an important conversation with Tech, she realized that they were all dealing with it in their own way.

Having cut ties with Cid, who had neglected them in their time of need on Ipsidon, the Bad Batch would work with the [pirate](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate") [Phee Genoa](/wiki/Phee_Genoa "Phee Genoa"), and Omega took an interest in her outlandish tales of adventure. They would eventually visit the remote paradise of [Pabu](/wiki/Pabu_island "Pabu island"), an island community that lay peacefully off the Empire's radar. Although Hunter wanted to stay on the island permanently and give Omega a peaceful life, they would learn that Crosshair had become an Imperial [prisoner](/wiki/Prisoner "Prisoner") following Echo's return with the intel. Echo presented them with Imperial information as well as the group receiving a transmission from Crosshair, who had momentarily escaped and warned them that the Empire was still hunting them. In fact, Omega specifically was still a person of interest to Imperial researcher [Doctor](/wiki/Doctor "Doctor") [Royce Hemlock](/wiki/Royce_Hemlock "Royce Hemlock"), who wanted to capture her to force Nala Se into working for the Empire's [Advanced Science Division](/wiki/Advanced_Science_Division "Advanced Science Division") project at [Tantiss Base](/wiki/Tantiss_Base "Tantiss Base").

The Batch made a plan to rescue Crosshair, traveling to the planet [Eriadu](/wiki/Eriadu "Eriadu") to locate Hemlock there and use him to find Crosshair. However, the [mission](/wiki/Bombing_of_Raven%27s_Peak "Bombing of Raven's Peak") proved disastrous, as they only escaped Imperial capture when Tech sacrificed himself and fell to his death. The whole squad was heartbroken, and Omega was devastated. Their return to Ord Mantell was equally calamitous, as Cid had sold them out to the Empire. Omega would be [captured](/wiki/Capture_of_Omega "Capture of Omega") and taken to Mount Tantiss where she would meet another female clone named [Emerie Karr](/wiki/Emerie_Karr "Emerie Karr"). On Mount Tantiss, Omega would be imprisoned and forced to be a lab assistant to Karr and Nala Se. Although Nala Se tried to protect Omega from involvement in her research by destroying her blood samples, eventually, her blood was tested and identified as of critical use for the Empire's [Project Necromancer](/wiki/Project_Necromancer "Project Necromancer"), causing the Kaminoan to facilitate Omega's escape. With the help of Nala Se's [datapad](/wiki/Datapad "Datapad"), Omega rescued Crosshair, who had also been imprisoned and tested on, and together, the two narrowly escaped [Mount Tantiss](/wiki/Mount_Tantiss "Mount Tantiss") and eventually reunited with the Bad Batch.

Omega was overjoyed to be reunited with her squad, and while Crosshair's return initially caused some friction, he was welcomed back as well. Soon after her return, Omega learned from intel gathered by Rex's Clone Underground that she was still one of the Empire's highest-priority targets and was being pursued by [Clone X troopers](/wiki/Clone_X_trooper "Clone X trooper") due to her [M-count](/wiki/Midi-chlorian "Midi-chlorian") levels, which had been determined through the blood testing. Omega was forced to lay low on Pabu while the others gathered information on why the Empire was so determined to find her. After Hunter and Wrecker did a mission with Fennec Shand in exchange for information about M-count, the former [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice") [Asajj Ventress](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress "Asajj Ventress") found them on Pabu to pass along the information they had sought, which was that M-count targets were potentially strong with [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force"). Despite the rest of the squad being distrusting of the former [Separatist](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") agent, Omega wanted to trust her and underwent several tests to see if she was in tune with the Force, as Ventress had suggested. However, the tests proved inconclusive.

After Ventress left Pabu, Hunter decided that Omega and the squad should leave the island, not wanting the Empire to also discover them there. However, it was too late. As they prepared to leave, an Imperial [division](/wiki/Division "Division") arrived, destroying the *Marauder* and ransacking the town from the top down. As Omega and the others hid, Omega decided that she would have to turn herself over to the Empire to prevent any more harm to the civilians of Pabu. She surrendered to CX-2, with Crosshair being tasked with planting a tracker on the assassin's ship. However, he failed to do so, and Omega was brought back to Tantiss without knowing that her brothers had no way to find her. Back at Tantiss, Doctor Hemlock introduced her to the other subjects in their experiment, several [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") children who were being kept in the [Tantiss vault](/wiki/Tantiss_vault "Tantiss vault"). At the same time that her brothers began an attack on Tantiss in an effort to free her, Omega plotted her own escape alongside her fellow child [prisoners](/wiki/Prisoner "Prisoner"). After aiding in the escape of the children and other imprisoned clones, Omega was briefly recaptured by Hemlock, though he was [killed](/wiki/Death "Death") as Hunter and Crosshair rescued her. After the escape from Tantiss, Omega and the rest of Clone Force 99 returned to Pabu, where they continued to live for many [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year"). At some point, Omega set out to join the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic") as a [pilot](/wiki/Pilot "Pilot").

## Biography

### Early life

 [![Omega's homeworld was the watery world of Kamino.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2c/TipocaCity-CC.png/revision/latest?cb=20130505022521) [![Omega's homeworld was the watery world of Kamino.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2c/TipocaCity-CC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130505022521)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2c/TipocaCity-CC.png/revision/latest?cb=20130505022521) 

Omega's homeworld was the watery world of Kamino.

 

Created in the [private laboratory](/wiki/Nala_Se%27s_private_lab "Nala Se's private lab") of [Kaminoan](/wiki/Kaminoan "Kaminoan") [scientist](/wiki/Scientist "Scientist") [Nala Se](/wiki/Nala_Se "Nala Se") on the[[7]](#cite_note-Return_to_Kamino-7) [extragalactic](/wiki/Extragalactic "Extragalactic") [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino") in the [star system](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") of the [same name](/wiki/Kamino_system "Kamino system"),[[8]](#cite_note-SWCL-8) Omega was an unmodified [clone](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") created with enhancements from the [genetic template](/wiki/DNA "DNA") of the [Mandalorian](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian") [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett").[[2]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-2) One of the Kaminoan's best-kept secrets,[[3]](#cite_note-GAR-3) she was one of only two clones that were pure genetic copies of the original Fett template—the other being [Boba Fett](/wiki/Boba_Fett "Boba Fett") (Alpha)—though Omega was unaware of this until later on in her childhood.[[2]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-2) Although she was a pure genetic copy, she was unlike Fett in that she was a [female](/wiki/Gender "Gender"). Omega worked as a medical assistant to Nala Se,[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1) the scientist who had enhanced her,[[9]](#cite_note-Dawn_Guide-9) enabling her to be present for the creation of [Clone Force 99](/wiki/Clone_Force_99 "Clone Force 99") in Se's private laboratory. Although she was present to see their mutations enhanced, the [clone commandos](/wiki/Clone_commando "Clone commando") were soon sent to be with the other [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper") the Kaminoans had made, leaving Omega alone once more.[[7]](#cite_note-Return_to_Kamino-7)

During the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars") between the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") and the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"), Clone Force 99—who took to calling themselves "the Bad Batch"—and the other clone [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") were sent across [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") to fight the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"),[[10]](#cite_note-The_Bad_Batch-10) while Omega remained on Kamino. Nevertheless, she remembered each member of the Bad Batch, namely [Hunter](/wiki/Hunter "Hunter"), [Wrecker](/wiki/Wrecker "Wrecker"), [Tech](/wiki/Tech "Tech"), and [Crosshair](/wiki/Crosshair "Crosshair"), even coming to learn that they had been joined by [CT-1409](/wiki/Echo "Echo") "Echo,"[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1) a [cyborg](/wiki/Cyborg "Cyborg") [Clone Corporal](/wiki/Clone_Corporal "Clone Corporal") who joined the [squad](/wiki/Squad "Squad") after the [Battle of Anaxes](/wiki/Battle_of_Anaxes "Battle of Anaxes")[[11]](#cite_note-Unfinished_Business-11) in [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY").[[12]](#cite_note-TCW_704_Date-12) However, she was never able to meet the Bad Batch throughout the course of the war. Stuck on Kamino, she did not feel like she fit in with the standard clone troopers who were stationed there.[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1)

### Rise of the Empire

#### Meeting the Bad Batch

:   "*I like you. You don't fit in around here either.*"
:   ―Omega, to the Bad Batch[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1)

 [![Omega meets Clone Force 99.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/Bad_batch_trailer_highlights.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210403232851) [![Omega meets Clone Force 99.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/Bad_batch_trailer_highlights.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20210403232851)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/Bad_batch_trailer_highlights.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210403232851) 

Omega meets Clone Force 99.

 

Omega finally had a chance to meet with the Bad Batch[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1) in 19 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system"),[[13]](#cite_note-Aftermath_Date-13) when they returned to Kamino after the [Conquest of Kaller](/wiki/Battle_of_Kaller "Battle of Kaller"), a conflict that had been suddenly ended by the execution of [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66") and the end of the Clone Wars. During the [Proclamation of the New Order](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order"), Omega stood by Nala Se's side and briefly made eye contact with the Bad Batch's leader, Hunter, only to vanish once he was distracted. Following the assembly, Omega approached the Bad Batch and introduced herself, addressing each member of the squad by name, much to their surprise. When they asked what she was doing on Kamino, Nala Se appeared and explained Omega's position as her medical assistant with a tendency to wander before leading her away.[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1)

 [![Omega demands an apology for the Bad Batch.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/OmegaDefendsBadBatch-Aftermath.png/revision/latest?cb=20220101060933) [![Omega demands an apology for the Bad Batch.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/OmegaDefendsBadBatch-Aftermath.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20220101060933)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/OmegaDefendsBadBatch-Aftermath.png/revision/latest?cb=20220101060933) 

Omega demands an apology for the Bad Batch.

 

Determined to grow closer to the Bad Batch, Omega decided to sit with them in the mess hall, which Tech noted was something that had never happened before. Unaware of her true nature as a clone, Hunter asked where her parents were. Omega barely had time to respond when [another clone trooper](/wiki/Unidentified_clone_trooper_(cafeteria) "Unidentified clone trooper (cafeteria)") made a passing remark, taunting the group by referring to them as the "Sad Batch." Taking offense, Omega threw [food](/wiki/Foodstuff "Foodstuff") at the clone and demanded he apologize. Hunter tried to de-escalate the situation, but Wrecker threw an entire tray of food at the clone trooper and started a brawl. Omega later tried to claim responsibility for the incident when the Bad Batch were called in for punishment, but Hunter refused, giving her a warning to stay away from their squad to avoid getting herself into trouble.[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1)

Omega later stood by Nala Se's side as she and the Kaminoan [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister "Prime Minister") [Lama Su](/wiki/Lama_Su "Lama Su") attempted to convince [Admiral](/wiki/Admiral "Admiral") [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin") to consider the Bad Batch as an asset to the new [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"). However, Tarkin was more concerned about the squad's tendencies to disregard orders, especially since they had failed to comply with Order 66. Though she failed to comprehend most of what she overheard, Omega got the impression that Tarkin did not trust clones. She tried to warn Hunter of this as the Bad Batch was about to depart on a [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Onderon_(Clone_Force_99) "Mission to Onderon (Clone Force 99)") to the[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1) planet[[14]](#cite_note-Onderon-14) [Onderon](/wiki/Onderon "Onderon"), but he dismissed her concerns. Nonetheless, she insisted on joining them, suspecting that it was no longer safe on Kamino. Hunter replied that change took time to get used to before departing with his squad.[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1)

 [![Omega is caught snooping in the Bad Batch's barracks](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/84/Shock-trooper-officer-attacks.png/revision/latest?cb=20220101223343) [![Omega is caught snooping in the Bad Batch's barracks](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/84/Shock-trooper-officer-attacks.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220101223343)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/84/Shock-trooper-officer-attacks.png/revision/latest?cb=20220101223343) 

Omega is caught snooping in the Bad Batch's barracks

 

While the squad was gone, Omega was instructed by Nala Se to stay in the medical wing. However, she decided to ignore these instructions and instead, accompanied by her [medical droid](/wiki/Medical_droid "Medical droid") companion [AZI-3](/wiki/AZI-345211896246498721347 "AZI-345211896246498721347"), made her way to the squad's [barracks](/wiki/Bad_Batch_barracks "Bad Batch barracks"). Omega looked around in awe at their gear, and although AZI-3 said that it was mostly worthless trinkets and scrap, Omega took interest it. AZI-3 reminded her that they should not have left the medical wing, but Omega told him that it was a research assignment, which excited the [droid](/wiki/Droid "Droid"). She took a special interest in a photograph of the squad, but was eventually discovered by a force of [clone shock troopers](/wiki/Imperial_shock_trooper "Imperial shock trooper") that had come to confiscate the squad's gear. She was incarcerated and given the designation [Prisoner](/wiki/Prisoner "Prisoner") 0219 while being held in a prison cell. She would later be joined in the custody by the Bad Batch, who were imprisoned following their refusal to act on Admiral Tarkin's orders to take out members of the rebel cell known as the [Partisans](/wiki/Partisans "Partisans"), who were being led by the human [Saw Gerrera](/wiki/Saw_Gerrera "Saw Gerrera") on Onderon.[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1)

#### Leaving home

 [![Omega helping the Bad Batch fight Crosshair](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ce/OmegaEscapeFromKamino-Aftermath.png/revision/latest?cb=20220101212145) [![Omega helping the Bad Batch fight Crosshair](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ce/OmegaEscapeFromKamino-Aftermath.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20220101212145)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ce/OmegaEscapeFromKamino-Aftermath.png/revision/latest?cb=20220101212145) 

Omega helping the Bad Batch fight Crosshair

 

Omega reminded them that she had warned them about Tarkin, but was surprised when Hunter told her that the squad had come back to help her. Omega reaffirmed her desire to go with them. However, Crosshair begins to dissent, accusing Hunter of being a poor leader for disobeying orders and for being "soft" for the way he acted on both Kaller and Onderon. After Hunter responded that Crosshair should focus on escape first and questioning his decision-making later, Crosshair angrily sat down. Omega then approached him and told the clone that she knew what he was going to do and asked him not to, also mentioning that it would not be his fault. Crosshair narrowed his eyes at her as shock troopers came to the cell and took him away.[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1)

As the remaining clones formulated an escape plan, Omega was tasked with sneaking out to deactivate the [ray shield](/wiki/Ray_shield "Ray shield") after Wrecker damaged a wall panel to allow her to escape the cell. The shock troopers eventually noticed that Omega was missing from the cell, but she then dropped down on them from the ceiling, recovering quickly to deactivate the ray shield and free the others, who incapacitated the troopers. As the group planned their next move, she told Hunter that their gear had been confiscated and was likely in the hangar, which they were able to recover. However, after the force geared up, Crosshair came to stop his former companions from leaving. He had been outfitted with new armor and had his [inhibitor chip](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip") effects magnified, forcing him to become loyal to the Empire. After a fight that involved Omega firing a [blaster](/wiki/DC-15A_blaster_carbine "DC-15A blaster carbine") for the first time and shooting Crosshair's weapon, the group escaped on the Bad Batch's [ship](/wiki/Starship "Starship"), the [*Marauder*](/wiki/Marauder_(Omicron-class) "Marauder (Omicron-class)").[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1)

As the group discussed their next move, Omega gave Wrecker his [tooka doll](/wiki/Tooka_doll "Tooka doll"), [Lula](/wiki/Lula "Lula"), which she had rescued during the battle, which greatly pleased him. She then made her way to the [cockpit](/wiki/Cockpit "Cockpit") to look out at [space](/wiki/Realspace "Realspace") for the first time. Eventually, the others moved to the cockpit as well, where Hunter let her sit, telling her to strap in as they made the jump to [hyperspace](/wiki/Hyperspace "Hyperspace") en route to the [Suolriep sector](/wiki/Suolriep_sector "Suolriep sector").[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1) Omega's escape proved problematic for the Kaminoans, who desired access to her unaltered genetic template.[[2]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-2) After Nala Se informed Lama Su of Omega's escape, Lama Su ordered her to not tell the Empire of the development.[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1)

#### The galaxy awaits

:   "*What is this?*"  
    "*That would be dirt.*"  
    "*It's amazing.*"
:   ―Omega and Tech[[15]](#cite_note-Cut_and_Run-15)

 [![Omega experiences dirt for the first time.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/OmegaDiscoversDirt-CaR.png/revision/latest?cb=20220102205911) [![Omega experiences dirt for the first time.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/OmegaDiscoversDirt-CaR.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220102205911)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/OmegaDiscoversDirt-CaR.png/revision/latest?cb=20220102205911) 

Omega experiences dirt for the first time.

 

Safely in hyperspace, Omega was amazed by the ship and explored every corner of it before falling asleep on the floor along with Wrecker. Deciding to visit an old ally, the group headed for[[15]](#cite_note-Cut_and_Run-15) the planet[[16]](#cite_note-Saleucami-16) [Saleucami](/wiki/Saleucami "Saleucami") to visit [Cut Lawquane](/wiki/Cut_Lawquane "Cut Lawquane"),[[15]](#cite_note-Cut_and_Run-15) a clone who had long since deserted the [Republic Army](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic").[[17]](#cite_note-The_Deserter-17) The *Marauder* landed a short distance away from [Lawquane's Farm](/wiki/Lawquane%27s_Farm "Lawquane's Farm") and the Bad Batch began to walk towards their homestead. When Omega walked out into the [sun](/wiki/Star "Star"), she took her first steps into the rest of the galaxy beyond Kamino. She was in awe, having never experienced any environment besides the perpetual overcast of Kamino. She was fascinated with her new surroundings, using her hand to scoop up some up dirt, which she had never seen before, and laughing. As the group marched on, Omega continued to marvel at her surroundings, gazing in wonder at the [plants](/wiki/Plant "Plant") and [butterflies](/wiki/Carrier_butterfly "Carrier butterfly"). When they reached the homestead, Hunter introduced Omega to Cut, his wife [Suu](/wiki/Suu_Lawquane "Suu Lawquane"), and his adopted children [Shaeeah](/wiki/Shaeeah_Lawquane "Shaeeah Lawquane") and [Jek](/wiki/Jek_Lawquane "Jek Lawquane"), who took her outside to play while the others talked inside.[[15]](#cite_note-Cut_and_Run-15)

 [![Omega unknowingly put herself in great danger.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a2/NexuStalksOmega-CaR.png/revision/latest?cb=20220102224625) [![Omega unknowingly put herself in great danger.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a2/NexuStalksOmega-CaR.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220102224625)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a2/NexuStalksOmega-CaR.png/revision/latest?cb=20220102224625) 

Omega unknowingly put herself in great danger.

 

Shaeeah and Jek showed Omega how to play catch with a ball, but Omega accidentally threw the ball beyond the fence. The two children told her not to worry about it and left the ball, going inside to pack, as the family was looking to leave Saleucami due to the growing Imperial presence. However, Omega decided to retrieve the ball herself, and, after traveling outside the perimeter fence, she drew the attention of a predatory [nexu](/wiki/Nexu "Nexu"). Hunter and Suu came out to rescue her, chasing off the creature. When Hunter began to berate her for being irresponsible, Cut stepped in. As Omega tearfully apologized, Cut hugged her and told her she was safe, carrying her back inside. Eventually, Omega sat in the gunner's nest of the *Marauder* in sadness. Meanwhile, Hunter and Suu discussed the incident, with Suu telling Hunter that children always had a way of getting into trouble and that they needed help staying safe. When Cut joined them, Hunter asked if the Lawquanes would be willing to take Omega with them, saying that she needed a peaceful life and not one of risk and danger.[[15]](#cite_note-Cut_and_Run-15)

Meanwhile, [Echo](/wiki/Echo "Echo") and Tech worked on forging [chain codes](/wiki/Chain_code "Chain code") for the Lawquanes so they could leave Saleucami in safety. Omega overheard Tech and Echo discussing how they were going to get the data for the codes as well as the disks, and Tech decided that if they allowed the *Marauder* to be impounded at the spaceport, they would be able to sneak in and access the what they needed. However, they decided to go about the plan without telling Hunter first, only alerting the squad leader once the [impound vessel](/wiki/Clone_impound_vessel "Clone impound vessel") was already taking the *Marauder* away. When Tech did communicate to Hunter about the plan, Omega listened to Hunter's angry reaction, telling Tech that turning in their ship was not his idea of a good plan. Tech replied that he had the situation under control, but when Hunter told him that Omega was on the ship, Tech and Echo were both surprised and concerned. Omega waved at the two aghast clones and smiled, telling Tech that she thought it was a good plan.[[15]](#cite_note-Cut_and_Run-15)

As the *Marauder* was placed in the [impound dock](/wiki/Saleucami_impound_dock "Saleucami impound dock"), a pair of clones boarded the vessel and searched it. Omega waited with Tech and Echo in a small space above the main cabin until they left. As Tech helped Omega down, Omega told them that the plan was working so far and asked how she could help. She was disappointed when Echo told her that she had experienced enough action so far and that they could handle it. She and Tech stayed together in the ship while Echo snuck in and stole chain codes for Tech to forge. When clone forces amassed near the ship, preventing Echo or Tech from passing the codes to Hunter, Wrecker, and the family, who had entered the spaceport and planned to pick them up before boarding the last [shuttle](/wiki/Shuttle "Shuttle"), Omega grabbed the codes and snuck out herself to deliver them, succeeding in bringing them to the group.[[15]](#cite_note-Cut_and_Run-15)

#### Choosing family

:   "*I know I made a mistake, and I have a lot to learn, but you don't have to get rid of me. I left Kamino with you. This is where I wanna be.*"
:   ―Omega, to Hunter[[15]](#cite_note-Cut_and_Run-15)

 [![Omega did not want to leave the Bad Batch](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/TBB-1x02-Omega.png/revision/latest?cb=20230103054314) [![Omega did not want to leave the Bad Batch](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/TBB-1x02-Omega.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/290?cb=20230103054314)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/TBB-1x02-Omega.png/revision/latest?cb=20230103054314) 

Omega did not want to leave the Bad Batch

 

However, when Omega noted that Tech had made an extra one, Hunter pulled her aside and told her that she would be going along with the family. Omega was shocked and asked if she had done something wrong, but Hunter just said that they could give her a happy and peaceful life that he and his squad could not. Omega protested that she wanted to stay with them, but Hunter told her it was for her own good before going to rendezvous with the rest of the Bad Batch, who had been discovered and were battling clone troopers in the impound dock. In sorrow, Omega went along through the gate with Cut and his family, whose forged passes were approved. As they were about to enter the spaceport, Omega stared longingly at the Bad Batch, who were battling Imperial forces as Echo attempted to free the *Marauder* from the magnetic [boot](/wiki/Boot_(technology) "Boot (technology)"), which was preventing them from taking off. Suu gently asked if Omega was ready to go, but Omega then decided to disobey Hunter and follow the Bad Batch, returning to the ship on her own.[[15]](#cite_note-Cut_and_Run-15)

 [![Hunter and Omega after the skirmish](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/CutAndRun.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210507105700) [![Hunter and Omega after the skirmish](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/CutAndRun.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20210507105700)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/CutAndRun.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210507105700) 

Hunter and Omega after the skirmish

 

As Echo removed the magnetic clamps from the *Marauder*, the squad prepared for takeoff. Wrecker asked Hunter where Omega was, unaware that Hunter had intended for her to go with the Lawquanes, but before he could explain, Omega shouted for them to wait as she scrambled towards the ship. She made it back onboard just in time and the squad lifted off and escaped. After the harrowing adventure, Omega approached Hunter on the ship and apologized for disobeying him, but also to reaffirm her desire to be among them. She said that she knew she had made a mistake when she had gone beyond the fence and put herself in danger, but said that one mistake did not mean that they had to get rid of her. Hunter replied that if it was what she wanted, then they would be glad to have her even if he still had much to learn about taking care of her.[[15]](#cite_note-Cut_and_Run-15)

#### Fitting in

:   "*I'll go with you.*"  
    "*No, that thing could be dangerous.*"  
    "*I'm part of this squad now too, right?*"
:   ―Omega convinces Hunter to let her come with him to reclaim their capacitor[[18]](#cite_note-Replacements-18)

After their escape from Saleucami, the group stayed on the move. They began to ration food as their supplies ran low. At one point, Omega was sitting on the floor looking at a [datapad](/wiki/Datapad "Datapad") when Hunter passed out [ration bars](/wiki/Ration_bar "Ration bar"). Omega offered hers to Wrecker when the bigger clone expressed his disappointment at the rationing, but Hunter reminded Wrecker that Omega did not even have a proper place to sleep. Just then, the *Marauder* dropped out of hyperspace due to the [power capacitor](/wiki/Capacitor "Capacitor"), with Tech stating that the ship was suffering from damage sustained on Saleucami. Wrecker helped Omega strap in as the shuttle crashed on the [Ordo Moon](/wiki/Ordo_Moon "Ordo Moon").[[18]](#cite_note-Replacements-18)

Omega remained in the cockpit as Echo and Tech went outside to replace the ship's [capacitor](/wiki/Capacitor "Capacitor"). When they returned, they reported that the hull was being damaged by something outside. Omega saw a [creature](/wiki/Ordo_Moon_Dragon "Ordo Moon Dragon") outside, and she yelled for the others to look. Tech deduced that the creature was an Ordo Moon Dragon, which fed on raw energy, and Echo checked the diagnostics and confirmed that the capacitor had been stolen. As Hunter prepared to go retrieve the device, Omega volunteered to come with him. Although he initially declined Omega's offer to join him, he relented and the pair donned [breath masks](/wiki/Breath_mask "Breath mask") and set off after the creature.[[18]](#cite_note-Replacements-18)

 [![Omega on the Ordo Moon.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/05/OmegaFindsSparky-Replacements.png/revision/latest?cb=20220105045853) [![Omega on the Ordo Moon.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/05/OmegaFindsSparky-Replacements.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20220105045853)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/05/OmegaFindsSparky-Replacements.png/revision/latest?cb=20220105045853) 

Omega on the Ordo Moon.

 

Omega followed Hunter as he used his enhanced senses to track the creature. As they traveled, Omega told Hunter that Crosshair should not be blamed for his actions and that he was powerless to stop himself. Hunter merely responded by saying that he did not blame Crosshair, but instead blamed himself. He eventually located the capacitor, but as Hunter tried to grab the part, the dragon attacked him and knocked off his breath mask. Omega grabbed his mask for him and put it back on his face, but not before Hunter fell unconscious. Omega contacted the others with a [comlink](/wiki/Comlink "Comlink"), but then decided to take Hunter's [blaster pistol](/wiki/DC-17_repeater_hand_blaster "DC-17 repeater hand blaster") and [flashlight](/wiki/Glowrod "Glowrod") and set off down the tunnels where the dragon disappeared. After some crawling, she located its den and the capacitor. When she returned to the surface, Hunter was worried for her safety, but Omega proudly displayed the part and reassured him that she was fine and said that she had completed their mission. Back onboard the ship, Wrecker showed Omega [her new room](/wiki/Omega%27s_Room "Omega's Room") he had set up for her in the gunner's nest. Omega expressed excitement and gratitude to Wrecker, telling the squad she had never had her own room before. Hunter then told her that she was now part of the squad.[[18]](#cite_note-Replacements-18)

### Pursued by dangerous foes

#### Exploring Pantora

:   "*Are you all right? You seem lost.*"  
    "*I got separated from my friends.*"  
    "*I can help with that. Not to worry. We'll find them.*"
:   ―Fennec Shand and Omega[[19]](#cite_note-Cornered-19)

As the Bad Batch discussed their next move, Omega was puzzled as to why Hunter suggested they go to the uninhabited [Idaflor](/wiki/Idaflor "Idaflor"), saying that they should explore and reminding them that she has never seen the galaxy like they had. After the group remembered they were out of rations and low on [fuel](/wiki/Fuel "Fuel"), Echo noted that he had overheard comm chatter that had their ship on the wanted list. The group decided to stop at the planet [Pantora](/wiki/Pantora "Pantora") to resupply, which Omega was happy to visit and explore.[[19]](#cite_note-Cornered-19)

 [![Omega initially trusted the deceitful Shand](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/Shand_and_Omega.png/revision/latest?cb=20220106043951) [![Omega initially trusted the deceitful Shand](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/Shand_and_Omega.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/335?cb=20220106043951)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/Shand_and_Omega.png/revision/latest?cb=20220106043951) 

Omega initially trusted the deceitful Shand

 

Upon landing, Wrecker and Tech stayed behind to scramble the ship's signature and refuel, while Omega joined Hunter and Echo on a quick supply run. As they made their way around [Ro Station](/wiki/Ro_Station "Ro Station"), Omega was again fascinated by a great variety of things she had never seen before. Noticing the citizens celebrating, she asked what they were doing, and Hunter said that they were celebrating the end of the war. As Hunter bartered with a [trader](/wiki/Unidentified_Gran_trader "Unidentified Gran trader"), Omega looked at a [clone trooper doll](/wiki/Clone_trooper_doll "Clone trooper doll") in the store. After she knocked over a container of them and was reprimanded by the merchant, she picked one up and showed it to Echo. When Hunter called Echo over to discuss selling him to the trader, who thought Echo was a droid due to his disguise, Omega noticed several [voorpaks](/wiki/Voorpak "Voorpak") being transported along the street. She ran over to them, but as she was petting them, one of them grabbed the doll out of her hands with its mouth, causing Omega to chase after them. However, she quickly became lost, and in a very unfamiliar environment, was frightened until a woman approached her. Unaware that the newcomer was a [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") named [Fennec Shand](/wiki/Fennec_Shand "Fennec Shand"),[[19]](#cite_note-Cornered-19) who had been hired by [Nala Se](/wiki/Nala_Se "Nala Se") to capture her and bring her back to Kamino,[[2]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-2) Omega gratefully accepted her help as Shand feigned compassion and promised to help her find her friends.[[19]](#cite_note-Cornered-19)

As they walked, Shand asked Omega if she was hungry. Omega said that she was, and Shand proceeded to swipe two fruits from a nearby stand. Omega pointed out that she had not paid for the fruit, but Shand smiled and said that it was alright to break the rules sometimes. Omega, noticing that her new companion was armed, asked if Shand was a soldier, but Shand merely said that the galaxy was a dangerous place to be alone in. Omega agreed, saying that she was glad to have her squad to help look after her.[[19]](#cite_note-Cornered-19)

Hunter, having deceived the merchant and made 3,000 [credits](/wiki/Galactic_Credit_Standard "Galactic Credit Standard") by selling Echo, eventually realized Omega was missing and after searching, located her walking with Shand. Sensing danger, he engaged Shand, telling Omega to run before he was head-butted and stunned. Shand gave chase, and as Omega made it into the maintenance tunnels, she ran in to Wrecker, whom Hunter had dispatched to locate her. When Shand caught up, Omega climbed a ladder to the surface as Wrecker fought Shand. However, Wrecker was quickly defeated, and as Omega found herself on a tower next to heavy speeder traffic, Shand had her cornered. As Omega ended up hanging off of the tower, Tech directed Hunter, who was riding a stolen [speeder bike](/wiki/Speeder_bike "Speeder bike"), towards her. Shand caught Omega as she fell and dropped her onto a transport before jumping on herself. After a fight with Hunter, the [speeder](/wiki/ComfortRide_passenger_airspeeder "ComfortRide passenger airspeeder") Shand had commandeered was destroyed by Hunter's [pyro denton explosive](/wiki/Pyro_denton_explosive "Pyro denton explosive"), and Hunter grabbed Omega before the group met up back at the ship and left Pantora. Identifying Shand as a bounty hunter, the Bad Batch realized someone had hired Shand to capture Omega.[[19]](#cite_note-Cornered-19)

#### Searching for answers

 [![The Bad Batch meet Cid](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/CidHome.png/revision/latest?cb=20220107040000) [![The Bad Batch meet Cid](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/CidHome.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/275?cb=20220107040000)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/CidHome.png/revision/latest?cb=20220107040000) 

The Bad Batch meet Cid

 

In the aftermath of their ordeal with the bounty hunter, Echo suggested they go to an old informant trusted by the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi"), [Cid](/wiki/Ciddarin_Scaleback "Ciddarin Scaleback"), to find out information on their pursuer. Onboard the *Marauder*, Omega was given a [comm device](/wiki/Wrist_comm "Wrist comm") and taught how to use it, which greatly excited her. Omega initially playfully used it to communicate to the squad despite being right next to them, but by the time they arrived on[[20]](#cite_note-Rampage-20) the planet[[21]](#cite_note-BMF_48-21) [Ord Mantell](/wiki/Ord_Mantell "Ord Mantell") to find Cid, she had become more serious, reciting the rules she had been given: don't wander off, pay attention to her surroundings, and use the comlink to contact them if she got into trouble. The group walked through [Ord Mantell City](/wiki/Ord_Mantell_City "Ord Mantell City") and soon entered a run-down [parlor](/wiki/Cid%27s_Parlor "Cid's Parlor") in search of Cid, and while the squad was initially told to get lost by a [Trandoshan](/wiki/Trandoshan "Trandoshan") woman, Omega deduced that the woman was actually Cid while the others discussed, an observation that Cid noticed and complemented.[[20]](#cite_note-Rampage-20)

Hunter quickly agreed to carry out a mission to [rescue](/wiki/Mission_to_Ord_Mantell_(Clone_Force_99) "Mission to Ord Mantell (Clone Force 99)") a child named [Muchi](/wiki/Muchi "Muchi") from a group of [Zygerrian](/wiki/Zygerrian "Zygerrian") [slavers](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery") on the other side of the planet. As they traveled there, Omega asked Echo about slavery. As Echo told her what it was, she frowned and said that she did not feel like that was right, to which Echo voiced his agreement. When they landed outside of [Old Ord Mantell City](/wiki/Old_Ord_Mantell_City "Old Ord Mantell City"), where the slavers were based, Omega was excited for their new mission, and was thus dejected when Hunter told her to stay with the ship as the squad moved in. Omega sat in the ship's cockpit and played with her doll, coloring it to resemble the Bad Batch's armor. As she showed her work to [Gonky](/wiki/Gonky_(Clone_Force_99) "Gonky (Clone Force 99)"), she heard voices outside. She grabbed a backpack and escaped the ship as a pair of Zygerrians searched inside. Looking through a pair of [macrobinoculars](/wiki/Macrobinoculars "Macrobinoculars"), she realized that her companions had been captured.[[20]](#cite_note-Rampage-20)

 [![Omega had to rescue her squad from the Zygerrians](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/OmegaSneaking-Rampage.png/revision/latest?cb=20220108011621) [![Omega had to rescue her squad from the Zygerrians](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/OmegaSneaking-Rampage.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/290?cb=20220108011621)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/OmegaSneaking-Rampage.png/revision/latest?cb=20220108011621) 

Omega had to rescue her squad from the Zygerrians

 

Omega snuck around the Zygerrian's camp and quickly made a plan, unlocking a cage that housed a [rancor](/wiki/Rancor "Rancor"). Although she was captured, she successfully set the beast loose, which caused havoc and gave Wrecker time to free the squad. Omega joined Echo in escorting the Zygerrians' three other prisoners, two [Falleen](/wiki/Falleen "Falleen") and a human, away while Hunter, Wrecker, and Tech went after the rancor, whom they had realized was Muchi. As they helped the others escape, Omega claimed a [Zygerrian energy bow](/wiki/Zygerrian_energy_bow "Zygerrian energy bow") off of the ground. Their mission successful, the team left to return to Cid, with Omega riding on top of Muchi. Once the rancor was taken away by[[20]](#cite_note-Rampage-20) [majordomo](/wiki/Majordomo "Majordomo")[[22]](#cite_note-CE-22) [Bib Fortuna](/wiki/Bib_Fortuna "Bib Fortuna"), who was representing Muchi's owner,[[20]](#cite_note-Rampage-20) the [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt") [crime lord](/wiki/Crime_lord "Crime lord")[[23]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-23) [Jabba Desilijic Tiure](/wiki/Jabba_Desilijic_Tiure "Jabba Desilijic Tiure"), Cid paid Hunter what she owed the squad and informed him about Shand, understanding that there had to be a reason a bounty hunter like her was chasing them.[[20]](#cite_note-Rampage-20)

#### First job for Cid

:   "*Take it easy, kid. I don't wanna hurt you, but I can't have you getting in the way.*"  
    "*You're the one in my way.*"
:   ―Rafa Martez and Omega[[24]](#cite_note-Decommissioned-24)

After their successful mission, Omega practiced shooting with her new [bow](/wiki/Omega%27s_Zygerrian_energy_bow "Omega's Zygerrian energy bow") in Cid's Parlor. Omega was proud to hit three out of twelve shots, which Echo said was just luck and that she needed to keep practicing. Omega was not strong enough to aim accurately on a consistent basis, and her efforts were not benefited by two other patrons, [Ketch](/wiki/Ketch "Ketch") and [Bolo](/wiki/Bolo "Bolo"), who began [gambling](/wiki/Gambling "Gambling") on her success. After missing two more times, Cid arrived, and after booting the two other aliens out of the parlor, briefed the group on their first [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_a_droid_decommissioning_facility "Mission to a droid decommissioning facility") for her: stealing a [tactical droid](/wiki/T-series_military_strategic_analysis_and_tactics_droid "T-series military strategic analysis and tactics droid") head on[[24]](#cite_note-Decommissioned-24) the planet[[25]](#cite_note-Corellia-25) [Corellia](/wiki/Corellia "Corellia"), which had valuable information for Cid to sell.[[24]](#cite_note-Decommissioned-24)

 [![Omega stops Rafa Martez from escaping with the tactical droid head.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c9/Omega_and_Rafa.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210608063100) [![Omega stops Rafa Martez from escaping with the tactical droid head.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c9/Omega_and_Rafa.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/290?cb=20210608063100)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c9/Omega_and_Rafa.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210608063100) 

Omega stops Rafa Martez from escaping with the tactical droid head.

 

The group landed and infiltrated a facility that was scrapping battle droids. Once they snuck past the [police droids](/wiki/Police_droid "Police droid") and got inside, Hunter stationed Omega and Wrecker as lookouts while he, Echo, and Tech moved in. Echo accessed a computer to discover that there was only one tactical droid inside, which Omega was able to spot on the conveyor belt. However, another individual disguised as a worker went in and stole the head. Omega alerted the others of this development before she found herself face-to-face with another person, [Rafa Martez](/wiki/Rafa_Martez "Rafa Martez"). Omega quickly drew her bow, causing Rafa to freeze and put her hands up. However, Rafa convinced her to lower the bow and talk it out, and when Omega did, Rafa knocked the bow out of her hands. The bow managed to discharge a single bolt that ruptured a steam pipe, alerting the facility workers to their presence. Rafa communicated with her sister [Trace](/wiki/Trace_Martez "Trace Martez"), who had the droid head, and as she went to meet up with her, Omega gave chase and told Hunter she was in pursuit. Meanwhile, the rest of the Bad Batch fought back against the police droids that began advancing on them.[[24]](#cite_note-Decommissioned-24)

 [![Omega with Hunter and their new allies](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/RafaOmegaHunter-Decommissioned.png/revision/latest?cb=20220108212748) [![Omega with Hunter and their new allies](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/RafaOmegaHunter-Decommissioned.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/275?cb=20220108212748)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/RafaOmegaHunter-Decommissioned.png/revision/latest?cb=20220108212748) 

Omega with Hunter and their new allies

 

Omega followed Rafa, who eventually got the head from Trace, but ended up losing it onto another conveyor belt. Omega and Trace raced for it, with Omega taking an alternate route that allowed her to reach it first. As she fled from Trace, Echo shut down the power and caused the conveyor belt to stop, which made Omega trip and lose the head. As she became pinned underneath debris, Trace swooped in and reclaimed the head. However, as Omega remained trapped and neared the edge of the conveyor that would tip her into a fire, Trace and Hunter came to save her.[[24]](#cite_note-Decommissioned-24)

The two groups decided to join forces and attempt to escape the growing number of police droids together, with Trace and Tech using the tactical droid head to command the other droids that were going to be scrapped into an army to battle the police droids. Omega used her energy bow to fire on the droids, also using her comm to contact Wrecker to help them. However, as the group fled the building, the tactical droid head was destroyed. The groups parted ways, with Omega waving goodbye and telling the sisters that they could visit them on Ord Mantell.[[24]](#cite_note-Decommissioned-24)

#### Meeting Rex

:   "*I've met many clones in my time, but never one like you.*"
:   ―Rex, upon meeting Omega[[26]](#cite_note-Battle_Scars-26)

The Bad Batch continued doing missions for Cid and earned enough credits to get by. Omega and Wrecker formed a tradition of purchasing and eating [Mantell Mix](/wiki/Mantell_Mix "Mantell Mix") after their missions. After a mission stealing a [lizard](/wiki/Lizard "Lizard") from the [Rhokai gang](/wiki/Rhokai_gang "Rhokai gang"), the pair went out for Mantell Mix as per usual, but when they returned, the former [Clone Captain](/wiki/Clone_Captain "Clone Captain") [Rex](/wiki/Rex "Rex") was seated with the others at the bar. Omega curiously took a close look at Rex when introduced, recognizing that he was a first generation clone and telling him as much. Rex was confused on how she knew that, and Omega responded that she could tell by the lines on his face.[[26]](#cite_note-Battle_Scars-26)

As the group continued talking, Wrecker asked Tech for treatment for his headache, a problem that had been ailing him for some time. When Rex learned that the squad had not had their inhibitor chips removed, he quickly stood up and backed away, placing Omega behind him and putting his hand on his blaster. Omega was distressed when Rex said that the four clones were a danger to themselves and to her. Hunter eventually got Rex to calm down and agreed to Rex's plan to remove their chips. Omega and the others met Rex on the planet [Bracca](/wiki/Bracca "Bracca"). As they overlooked a downed [*Venator*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Unidentified_Venator-class_Star_Destroyer_(Clone_Force_99) "Unidentified Venator-class Star Destroyer (Clone Force 99)"), Rex explained his plan to find the ship's medical bay and remove their inhibitor chips there.[[26]](#cite_note-Battle_Scars-26)

 [![Omega tries to hide from Wrecker](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/51/Omega-hiding-from-Wrecker.png/revision/latest?cb=20220109195042) [![Omega tries to hide from Wrecker](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/51/Omega-hiding-from-Wrecker.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20220109195042)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/51/Omega-hiding-from-Wrecker.png/revision/latest?cb=20220109195042) 

Omega tries to hide from Wrecker

 

Omega followed as Rex led the group inside the ship, avoiding the patrols of the local group in power, the [Scrapper Guild](/wiki/Scrapper_Guild "Scrapper Guild"). They eventually located the medbay, but as Wrecker prepared to be the first to be treated, his chip activated. After knocking out Tech, he chased Rex, Echo, and Hunter out of the room, with Omega staying as instructed to look after Tech. However, Omega decided to grab Wrecker's [blaster](/wiki/DC-17m_Interchangeable_Weapon_System "DC-17m Interchangeable Weapon System") and fire at him. As Wrecker had incapacitated the other three, he chased after Omega. She slipped underneath a door, but Wrecker forced the door open with ease. Omega tried to hide, but she was discovered. However, she was saved by Rex, who stunned Wrecker just as she was discovered.[[26]](#cite_note-Battle_Scars-26)

 [![Omega and Wrecker continue their tradition](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fe/OmegaForgivesWrecker-BS.png/revision/latest?cb=20220109200630) [![Omega and Wrecker continue their tradition](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fe/OmegaForgivesWrecker-BS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220109200630)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fe/OmegaForgivesWrecker-BS.png/revision/latest?cb=20220109200630) 

Omega and Wrecker continue their tradition

 

As Wrecker was prepared for the chip removal once again, the procedure finished, but Wrecker did not immediately wake up. Rex suggested Hunter take Omega topside to get some air, but Omega firmly said that she would stay with Wrecker. The group sat around waiting, with Omega falling asleep, but she was wakened by Wrecker's gentle hand on her head. Omega excitedly welcomed him back, and as the others prepared to have their chips removed, Wrecker pulled Omega aside and apologized for what he had done, feeling bad that he was unable to control himself against the chip's effects. Omega told him that she didn't blame him, and pulled out some leftover Mantell Mix, telling Wrecker that their mission was a success and that they could not break their tradition. Rex departed that evening.[[26]](#cite_note-Battle_Scars-26)

The next morning, Omega would join Echo and Wrecker back on the surface, where Wrecker began to teach her how to disarm bombs. Omega initially felt good about her ability to do so, but when Wrecker handed her a pair of cutters and told her to disarm the bomb that he had just activated and would detonate in the next ten seconds, Omega panicked and failed to do so, running before it exploded. However, it turned out to only be a [smoke bomb](/wiki/Smoke_grenade "Smoke grenade"). The pair met up with Echo to return to the group, but Echo noticed that they were being watched by the Scrapper Guild. He and Wrecker attacked the trio of scavengers, eventually stunning all three of them. When the Batch met up, Echo suggested they leave, but Tech and Hunter decided that the group would go to salvage weapons from the armory and data from the bridge that would settle their debt with Cid. Omega asked what to do with their three prisoners, but Hunter promised that they would be in and out before they even woke up.[[27]](#cite_note-Reunion-27)

In the artillery bay, Omega found a chest of explosives while Wrecker found several [proton torpedoes](/wiki/Proton_torpedo "Proton torpedo"). Omega asked if he would teach her how to arm one of the torpedoes, but Wrecker smiled and said that they were all his. Then, Tech, who was on the bridge, commed Omega to come to him, and she arrived to help Tech copy the master drive. As Omega looked out the viewport at the wreckage of several Republic ships, she asked Tech what the war was like. When Tech gave a straightforward technical answer, Omega asked him what the war was really like. Tech did not elaborate, but when Omega asked why a button was blinking, Tech got up and told her it was the [proximity sensor](/wiki/Proximity_sensor "Proximity sensor"). While Tech guessed it was a malfunction, a trio of [Imperial shuttles](/wiki/Nu-class_attack/transport_shuttle "Nu-class attack/transport shuttle") flew by and landed. Tech warned Hunter, who joined them on the bridge. Seeing Crosshair, Omega followed Hunter and Tech back down to Echo and Wrecker as they worked out a plan to escape.[[27]](#cite_note-Reunion-27)

#### Discovered

:   "*Omega. Get behind me.*"
:   ―Hunter, to Omega, as the bounty hunter Cad Bane approaches[[27]](#cite_note-Reunion-27)

 [![The Bad Batch sneak through the ship with their new supplies](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b2/CloneForce99-Reunion.png/revision/latest?cb=20220110010501) [![The Bad Batch sneak through the ship with their new supplies](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b2/CloneForce99-Reunion.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/275?cb=20220110010501)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b2/CloneForce99-Reunion.png/revision/latest?cb=20220110010501) 

The Bad Batch sneak through the ship with their new supplies

 

Carrying the minimal supplies they had taken, the Bad Batch moved through the corridors towards the hangar. However, when Tech patched into their comm systems and realized that the Empire's plan was to push them towards the hangar, they changed course towards the artillery deck. However, there, they were nonetheless surrounded. Crosshair told his men to aim at Omega, and while she hid behind Hunter, Tech fired the cannons, destabilizing the deck and sending debris crashing down around them. The group escaped to the [ion engine](/wiki/Ion_engine "Ion engine") chamber, but they were eventually pinned down there as well, with one of Crosshair's men starting the engines while the main force trapped them inside. Tech came up with a quick plan to plant the explosives they had, and Omega reached one of the higher points on the cylinder, sending the part of the engine they were occupying crashing to the ground so they avoided being incinerated. There, Hunter and Omega were separated from the others, but Hunter told the group to meet back at the ship.[[27]](#cite_note-Reunion-27)

Back at the ship, Omega and Hunter found a group of clone troopers had been killed. Hunter examined the bodies and determined there was someone else there, and the pair watched as the bounty hunter [Cad Bane](/wiki/Cad_Bane "Cad Bane") emerged from his ship.[[27]](#cite_note-Reunion-27) Bane had been hired by Lama Su to retrieve Omega so her genetic material could be used to create new and improved clones for the Empire.[[2]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-2) Hiding behind Hunter, Omega listened as Bane said that, after killing so many clones over the [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year"), it had become easy for him. Omega deduced that Bane was a bounty hunter, and as Bane demanded that she be turned over, Hunter refused. After the two engaged in a standoff, Omega watched in horror as Hunter was defeated and shot in the chest. Omega tried to fight back, but she was quickly disarmed by Bane's droid companion [Todo 360](/wiki/Todo_360 "Todo 360") and stunned by the bounty hunter before being taken.[[27]](#cite_note-Reunion-27)

#### Escape on Bora Vio

 [![Omega cuffed by Bane](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/Cad_Bane_drags_Omega.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210627185506) [![Omega cuffed by Bane](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/Cad_Bane_drags_Omega.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20210627185506)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/Cad_Bane_drags_Omega.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210627185506) 

Omega cuffed by Bane

 

Omega was placed in a cell on [Bane's ship](/wiki/Justifier "Justifier") with a [ray shield](/wiki/Ray_shield "Ray shield") blocking her exit. She tried to learn who her captors were, but Bane ignored her questions and told her to be quiet and cooperate. However, she was able to escape when she tricked Todo 360 into letting her out to help him repair his leg. Omega searched for her comm device as Bane's ship landed at a [facility](/wiki/Bora_Vio_cloning_facility "Bora Vio cloning facility") on the planet [Bora Vio](/wiki/Bora_Vio "Bora Vio"), fleeing the ship after Bane went into the hold to look for Todo, who had been unresponsive. Omega contacted the Bad Batch, but she did not know where she was and the group could not pinpoint her location. Tech tried to talk her through how to help them find her, but Bane caught up to her and cuffed her, stomping on and destroying her comm device.[[2]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-2)

As Omega was forcefully dragged by Bane, he spotted the corpse of [Taun We](/wiki/Taun_We "Taun We"), the Kaminoan who Lama Su had dispatched to meet Bane and deliver his payment. Omega recognized her and was horrified. Taking cover, Omega watched as Bane and Fennec Shand, the bounty hunter who had pursued her on Pantora, faced off. As the two fought, Omega fled, finding herself in a room with several clones in tubes. She was able to access a computer to send out a signal that her team would eventually recognize, but Shand soon caught up to her. Shand told her that she was trying to help her, but Omega pointed out that she had said the same thing on Pantora. Unknown to Omega, Shand had been sent by Nala Se to prevent her from being brought to Lama Su. They were interrupted by Todo, who Shand quickly smashed against one of the tubes and incapacitated. Returning to the computer, Omega caused the tube to crack and eventually spilled its contents onto Shand, giving Omega time to escape.[[2]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-2)

 [![Omega trying to evade Bane and Shand](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/Rescue_of_Omega.png/revision/latest?cb=20220111013313) [![Omega trying to evade Bane and Shand](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/Rescue_of_Omega.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20220111013313)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/Rescue_of_Omega.png/revision/latest?cb=20220111013313) 

Omega trying to evade Bane and Shand

 

Omega tried to descend a ladder, but she was hampered by her handcuffs and eventually hounded by Todo. Omega ended up jumping on top of the butler droid and descending rapidly to a platform. Omega noticed several [Kaminoan flight pods](/wiki/Kaminoan_flight_pod "Kaminoan flight pod") and used one to escape the facility. Just as the engines began to fail, the *Marauder* located her and picked her up, and Omega was reunited with the team. A tearful Omega hugged her companions, asking why the Kaminoans were sending so many hunters after her. Echo told Hunter that he had to tell her what they had learned about her, and he explained she was an unmodified clone, making her important to the Kaminoans. That night, Omega and Hunter sat in the cockpit. Omega said that she could not sleep because she was thinking about the Kaminoans and how they could not fight off all of the hunters that would always be after her. Hunter reassured her and promised that she would never go back to Kamino, making her smile. Shand later reported Omega's escape to Nala Se and asked if she should continue tracking her, but the Kaminoan was satisfied that Omega was free from Lama Su.[[2]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-2)

### Part of the squad

#### Left out

:   "*But th-the mission. I'm part of the squad too.*"  
    "*Then following orders shouldn't be a problem.*"
:   ―Omega and Hunter[[28]](#cite_note-Common_Ground-28)

Omega happily returned to Ord Mantell with the rest of the Bad Batch, eating Mantell Mix while riding on Wrecker's shoulders. As they made their way back to Cid's, Tech announced that they should try to lay low since Omega had two bounty hunters after her. She offered some of the snacks to Echo while Hunter whispered to Wrecker that he thought Omega needed a break after what she had been through. Speaking with Cid, the group was offered a job to help rescue [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") [Avi Singh](/wiki/Avi_Singh "Avi Singh") from Imperial prison on his planet, [Raxus Secundus](/wiki/Raxus_Secundus "Raxus Secundus"). Hunter refused the job, saying they would not help a former [Separatist](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"), but his main rationale was that he did not want to endanger Omega's safety on an Imperial-occupied planet. Hunter begrudgingly decided to accept the job and leave Omega behind with Cid. Omega was enthusiastic about their new mission, and was saddened when Hunter notified her that she would not be coming with them. Omega pleaded her case, saying that she was a part of the squad too, but Hunter countered by saying that as a member of the squad, she should have no problem following orders. Omega groaned but complied, and as soon as the others departed on their [mission](/wiki/Extraction_on_Raxus "Extraction on Raxus"), Cid put her to work cleaning her parlor.[[28]](#cite_note-Common_Ground-28)

As Omega moped around the parlor, Cid eventually came over and, after telling her to stop dampening the mood, asked her what was wrong. Omega told her that she was worried about her friends before stating that it was not fair that she was not allowed to go on the mission with them. Cid responded that life was not fair and that maybe if she was not so helpless she wouldn't have been left behind in her care. Omega was hurt by her words and stalked away.[[28]](#cite_note-Common_Ground-28)

 [![Omega playing dejarik with Cid](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ec/CidOmegaDejarik-CG.png/revision/latest?cb=20220111211631) [![Omega playing dejarik with Cid](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ec/CidOmegaDejarik-CG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/275?cb=20220111211631)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ec/CidOmegaDejarik-CG.png/revision/latest?cb=20220111211631) 

Omega playing dejarik with Cid

 

Later, Omega watched as Cid squared off against [Ketch](/wiki/Ketch "Ketch") and [Bolo](/wiki/Bolo "Bolo"), two frequent patrons in the cantina, in a game of [dejarik](/wiki/Dejarik "Dejarik"). Omega raised her opinion on what move Cid should play, and was promptly ignored, which allowed her opponents to capitalize. Cid groaned and asked Omega what move she should play now, and after she listened to her, pulled out the victory. Cid asked Omega how she knew what to do, and Omega responded by saying that she was good at strategy games. Cid asked if she was good enough to make her some money, offering her thirty percent of the cut, but Omega smirked and replied that she wanted sixty. Eventually, the two faced several other opponents, winning games and drawing a large crowd of various aliens to the parlor to watch. By the time Hunter, Wrecker, Echo, and Tech returned with the rescued Senator Singh and [his droid](/wiki/GS-8 "GS-8"), Omega had made enough money to pay off the Batch's debt to Cid. Although Hunter was not happy that Omega had drawn so much attention to herself, he was pleased by her earnings and challenged her to a game, saying that if she won, she would not be left out of any other missions. Omega excitedly took her seat, and when Hunter asked her if she was ready for it, she confidently said that he was the one who needed to make sure he was ready to face her.[[28]](#cite_note-Common_Ground-28)

#### Helping a new friend

:   "*Make a new friend?*"  
    "*She's kinda strange.... I like her. Did you know flying's about a feeling?*"
:   ―Hunter and Omega, regarding Hera Syndulla[[29]](#cite_note-Devil's_Deal-29)

 [![Omega meeting Hera Syndulla](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/31/Omega_meets_Hera_Syndulla.png/revision/latest?cb=20220112053228) [![Omega meeting Hera Syndulla](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/31/Omega_meets_Hera_Syndulla.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20220112053228)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/31/Omega_meets_Hera_Syndulla.png/revision/latest?cb=20220112053228) 

Omega meeting Hera Syndulla

 

Omega and the squad would soon take the *Marauder* to deliver weapons to a group of [Twi'leks](/wiki/Twi%27lek "Twi'lek") on behalf of Cid, agreeing to meet on [third moon](/wiki/Ryloth%27s_third_moon "Ryloth's third moon") of the planet [Ryloth](/wiki/Ryloth "Ryloth"). While the others made the deal, Omega gave the young Twi'lek girl [Hera Syndulla](/wiki/Hera_Syndulla "Hera Syndulla") a tour of the ship. Omega showed her the cockpit, where she learned that Hera wanted to become a pilot. Omega was fascinated by her ambitions to fly, and after showing the other girl her room in the gunner's nest, Omega gave Hera their comm channel to contact them. She waved goodbye when the group of Twi'leks departed.[[29]](#cite_note-Devil's_Deal-29)

Shortly after departing from the weapons deal, the Batch received a transmission from Hera, who told them that her parents had been captured by the Empire and she needed their help, saying she will send them [coordinates](/wiki/Galactic_coordinates "Galactic coordinates"). Hunter, surprised Hera had their comm channel to contact them, questioned Omega as to why she gave it to her, but Omega simply said that it was for emergencies and that they needed to help her. Hunter shook his head and said that they could not help everyone, but Omega pointed out that, in fact, that was what soldiers do. The group reluctantly decided to meet Hera on Ryloth.[[30]](#cite_note-Rescue_on_Ryloth-30)

After hearing Hera's plan, listening to her offer to pay them, and scouting out the enemy forces, Hunter decided that he did not want to go about helping her. Omega was angered by Hunter's choice, saying that they needed to help her. Hunter said that he was being strategic and that he was not going to risk the squad, but Omega pleaded with him, saying that Hera was just trying to protect her family, just as she would do for any of them. As Hunter pondered, Omega consulted Hera, telling her that Hunter meant well and would come around. Hera asked why she trusted him, to which Omega said that he, as well as the others, were all her brothers. Finally, Omega said that if Hera could use her local knowledge to form a plan, they might be able to convince Hunter to help her. Omega and Hera concocted a strategy and introduced it to the squad: they proposed they split up to attack the refinery to draw away Imperial reinforcements away while the others infiltrated the city to rescue Hera's parents. Hunter decided to follow Hera's lead, ordering Tech and Wrecker to mount the attack on the refinery while he and Echo snuck into the city.[[30]](#cite_note-Rescue_on_Ryloth-30)
