As Karr activated a panel in the cell to send the blood sample to the labs, Omega took her chance to snag one of Karr's instruments from her, stowing the pointy tool in her sleeve. Karr left without noticing, and Omega soon spotted her above in the observation deck. Sitting in the center of the vault with the other children, Omega began to formulate a plan. She asked how often the droids came to check their vitals, and Eva told her that it was twice a day, after meals. Omega asked if the troopers ever came inside, and Jax hardened and said that they only entered when there was trouble. Eva explained Jax's recent escape attempt, and Jax insisted that there was no way out and that the children were never going home. Omega told them that she had escaped before and that she could do it again, promising that she would help them all escape. Jax then joined them at their table as Omega showed them a map of the base that she had made with the toys, showing them the pneumatic tube system in the walls that the blood samples were sent through and showing them the tool she had taken, saying she was going to find out where the tubes went. Jax was concerned that she would not be able to inspect the tubes without being seen, but Omega merely smiled and said that she liked a challenge.[[66]](#cite_note-Breach-66)

 [![Doctor Scalder suspected Omega was up to something](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/IntotheBreachTBB-AltThumbnail.png/revision/latest?cb=20240418231307) [![Doctor Scalder suspected Omega was up to something](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/IntotheBreachTBB-AltThumbnail.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240418231307)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/IntotheBreachTBB-AltThumbnail.png/revision/latest?cb=20240418231307) 

Doctor Scalder suspected Omega was up to something

 

Soon after, Omega took her chance to inspect the tubes, chiseling through and opening a passage. As she inspected it, she accidentally bumped several other tiles that made up the wall, which fell to the ground in a clatter. However, she was quickly able to replace the tiles and lay down on her cot before Doctor [Scalder](/wiki/Scalder "Scalder"), who had been suspicious of Omega, entered her cell. When she found nothing, Omega asked Scalder what was wrong, causing the Doctor to grunt and leave. Omega returned to the tables and told the other children that she had found a way out.[[66]](#cite_note-Breach-66)

Omega waited for her chance to continue to explore the passageway she had uncovered. Later, Omega was sitting with the other children when she heard the distinct boom of laser cannons and felt the room shake. The other children were concerned and asked what was going on, and Omega smiled and told them that her brothers had found her. They witnessed the Imperial scientists hurry around the observation deck as the base went into lockdown, and Omega, seeing her chance to inspect their potential escape route, told the others to cover for her. Sami asked what that meant, and Omega explained that they only had to keep the droids busy and stall them if they came to collect their samples so as to give her time to return. Although her companions did not seem confident, Omega decided to trust them and sneaked away from Scalder's watchful eye.[[67]](#cite_note-Flash-67)

 [![Omega cleverly found an opportunity to attempt an escape](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/FlashStrikeTBB-Thumbnail.png/revision/latest?cb=20240424224129) [![Omega cleverly found an opportunity to attempt an escape](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/FlashStrikeTBB-Thumbnail.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/275?cb=20240424224129)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/FlashStrikeTBB-Thumbnail.png/revision/latest?cb=20240424224129) 

Omega cleverly found an opportunity to attempt an escape

 

Once again removing the tiles, Omega climbed inside the passageway that accompanied the pneumatic tube system. She was able to climb up and around, watching lifts rattle past her at high speeds. She began to explore and, after some time, discovered a [sublevel containment chamber](/wiki/Sublevel_containment_chamber "Sublevel containment chamber"), where a massive Zillo Beast was being held in a water-filled [tank](/wiki/Zillo_tank "Zillo tank"). Omega watched the beast be subjected to an [ion cannon](/wiki/NNJ-40_%22Thunderbolt%22_long-range_ion_cannon "NNJ-40 \"Thunderbolt\" long-range ion cannon"). Deciding that she had scouted enough, she quickly retraced her steps and returned to her cell, just in time for her vitals to be taken. After Scalder and the droids left, the others anxiously awaited to hear what she had discovered. Omega once again smiled confidently and said that she had an escape plan.[[67]](#cite_note-Flash-67)

#### The plan

With the promise of her brothers finding her, Omega was confident that she and the others would be able to escape, and despite the hesitation of the others, she decided that it was time to set her plan in motion. Taking their positions, Eva and Jax approached one of the medical droids and distracted it as Omega used her stolen tool to temporarily incapacitate it. Moving it to the cell, Sami sat at the center tables to be alert for danger as Omega attempted to reprogram the droid. Sami alerted them that Dr. Scalder was on the way, and as Jax and Eva told her to hurry, Omega was able to finish the job and stand at attention when Scalder arrived. The doctor accused them of plotting, but Omega insisted they were with the droid as the reprogrammed droid moved behind Scalder and injected her with sedative. As she collapsed unconscious, Omega and the others quickly made for Omega's cell, and after she opened the passageway to the pneumatic system, they set off together.[[6]](#cite_note-Cavalry-6)

 [![Omega guided her newfound companions to safety](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/Omega-Cavalry.png/revision/latest?cb=20240508044151) [![Omega guided her newfound companions to safety](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/Omega-Cavalry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/275?cb=20240508044151)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/Omega-Cavalry.png/revision/latest?cb=20240508044151) 

Omega guided her newfound companions to safety

 

With the others following her the pneumatic system, Omega retraced her steps to the sublevel containment chamber. There, she instructed her companions to wait while she snuck towards the control console. Arriving undetected, she released the beast, causing chaos amongst the Imperial ranks. After the beast laid waste to the stormtroopers that had been sent to stop it, it climbed up to a hangar and broke out of the facility, escaping into the jungle. Once it was safe, Omega had the others follow her towards a ladder that she thought would lead to the exit the beast had created. Jax was nervous about the proposition of climbing, saying that he was afraid of heights and admitted that he would not make a good soldier. Omega comforted him, telling him about her brother Wrecker, who was also afraid of heights, but was one of the bravest people she knew. They then proceeded to climb, with Omega leading the way.[[6]](#cite_note-Cavalry-6)

Reaching the hangar undetected, the group snuck through the wreckage that the Zillo had left in its wake until they were cornered by stormtroopers. However, Omega watched as one of the troopers fired on the other two before they could call it in, and was surprised to see Echo take off his helmet.[[6]](#cite_note-Cavalry-6) He had snuck into the facility to locate her.[[67]](#cite_note-Flash-67) He was also being accompanied by Karr, who had decided to turn on the Empire and help Echo rescue the children. Echo told Omega that the rest of the Batch had been captured. Locating a shuttle, Echo and Omega instructed Karr to take the shuttle and the children to safety, with Echo giving her coordinates to head for. Jax asked why Omega wasn't coming with them, and Omega responded that she could not leave without helping her squad as well as the other clones. The children hugged Omega goodbye and she promised she would see them again soon. Karr put her hand on Omega's shoulder, telling her to be safe and giving the younger clone her datapad, saying it would help them move through the facility.[[6]](#cite_note-Cavalry-6)

#### The mission

:   "*You ready?*"  
    "*Let's complete the mission.*"
:   ―Echo and Omega[[6]](#cite_note-Cavalry-6)

Accompanying Echo to the detention block, freeing the clones there. Omega was happily surprised to find Nala Se there as well. However, Hunter, Wrecker, and Crosshair were nowhere to be found. As Omega helped to pass out weapons to the liberated clones, Echo spoke with one of the other prisoners about the potential whereabouts of the rest of the Batch. The clone suggested they could be in the [training room](/wiki/Tantiss_Base_training_room "Tantiss Base training room"), and Omega realized that she knew where to find the room. As they prepared to head there, the former Imperial Admiral Rampart, who had also been imprisoned following his role in the Bad Batch finding their way to Tantiss, declared that they had to leave and that it was foolish to stay. Echo instead appealed to the liberated clones, saying that they had every right to want their freedom, but that he and Omega needed their help to make sure the rest of their squad made it out. The clones did not hesitate in vowing to help them. As they prepared to leave, Nala Se told Omega that the only way she could be free is if Hemlock and all of his research was destroyed. Omega agreed and said that they could go to the lab right away, but Nala Se insisted that her place was with the other clones, so Omega gave her Karr's datapad before joining the others.[[6]](#cite_note-Cavalry-6)

Echo suggested that Omega use the pneumatic tube system to see inside the training room, so Omega, taking a comm, climbed inside and got into position. Spotting her three brothers, she alerted Echo, who stormed into the base of the room with the other clones. As the fighting commenced, Omega snuck into the raised center of the room to free the others. However, as she pressed the buttons on the console to release the restraints binding her brothers, she was stopped by Hemlock, who disdainfully commented that loyalty was the clone's weakness. Omega was helpless to watch as Hemlock's other clone assassins caused heavy casualties to the escaped prisoners down below, and Hemlock also released a gas that caused the clones to drop unconscious to the floor.[[6]](#cite_note-Cavalry-6)

Meanwhile, unbeknownst to Omega, Nala Se had used a detonator to destroy the lab, her last action after Rampart had fatally shot her. The Kaminoan, Rampart, and all of Hemlock's work was destroyed. As Scorch alerted Hemlock of the development, Omega taunted him that his research had been lost. Hemlock retorted that they still had her, and Omega coolly replied that she had her brothers. Wrecker, who had recovered enough to finish breaking out of his restraints, roared and sent a large piece of metal flying at the group, scattering them. As Hunter and Crosshair joined the fight, Hemlock cuffed Omega to his wrist using [magnetic binders](/wiki/Magnetic_binders "Magnetic binders") and, telling his clone assassins to deal with them, left with Scorch and headed for the exit.[[6]](#cite_note-Cavalry-6)

Omega was dragged outside into the rain by Hemlock, who headed towards the end of a long bridge that housed a landing platform. As the Doctor remotely summoned a CX Dagger vessel, Hunter and Crosshair appeared, eliminating Scorch. Hemlock used Omega as a human shield, holding his blaster to her head. Omega was convinced that Hemlock would not hurt her, but Hemlock nonetheless threatened her in an attempt to get the clones to lower their weapons. Omega, still cuffed to Hemlock, flashed the stolen tool that had helped her escape the vault. Hunter, understanding her signal, told Crosshair to be ready to fire on Hemlock. Omega stabbed the tool into Hemlock's arm, and, as the Imperial scientist pulled away, Omega ducked and Crosshair fired, breaking the cuffs. They then finished off Hemlock, sending him toppling off the platform and plummeting to his death. As Hunter and Crosshair wearily collapsed, Omega ran to them, hugging them both. They then joined Echo, Wrecker, and freed clones on a *Rho*-class shuttle, leaving Tantiss for good.[[6]](#cite_note-Cavalry-6)

#### Finally free

:   "*We've all fought enough battles for one lifetime. Now we get to choose who we want to be.*"  
    "*Like what?*"  
    "*Whatever we want, kid. Whatever we want.*"
:   ―Hunter and Omega[[6]](#cite_note-Cavalry-6)

 [![Omega and her squad at peace](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f7/Omega-Hunter-At-Peace.png/revision/latest?cb=20240503182342) [![Omega and her squad at peace](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f7/Omega-Hunter-At-Peace.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/275?cb=20240503182342)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f7/Omega-Hunter-At-Peace.png/revision/latest?cb=20240503182342) 

Omega and her squad at peace

 

The clones returned to Pabu, where the island community was recovering from the Imperial incursion. There, the clones were fed and offered the chance to stay on Pabu if they wanted to. Under the shining sun, Omega and Hunter sat beneath the weeping maya tree, watching Eva, Jax, Sami, and Bayrn walk with Deke, Mox, and Stak. Omega asked how long it would take to find their families, and Hunter promised that he and Rex were working on it. Omega wondered about what the clones would do, and Hunter told her that some would stay on Pabu, and others would choose their own path elsewhere. Echo would help settle several of them on Pantora, and also offered Emerie Karr the opportunity to help the Clone Underground, which she accepted. As Echo prepared the group to leave, he acknowledged Omega and Hunter before boarding the ship. Hunter concluded his thoughts by saying that the clones, including them, had fought enough battles and could now choose what they wanted to be. Omega asked what they would choose, and Hunter smiled and said they could choose whatever they wanted. Joined by Wrecker and Crosshair, Omega closed her eyes and rested her head on Hunter's shoulder, free and safe at last.[[6]](#cite_note-Cavalry-6)

### A new calling

:   "*The Rebellion needs pilots now more than ever. I made my choice, Hunter. I want to do more.*"  
    "*And we want to keep you safe.*"  
    "*You have. But I'm not a kid anymore. You don't have to worry about me.*"  
    "*You're* our *kid, Omega. You always will be.*"
:   ―Omega and Hunter[[6]](#cite_note-Cavalry-6)

 [![Omega was ready to leave Pabu and embark on her own galactic adventures](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b3/Epilogue-Omega-Hunter.png/revision/latest?cb=20240503182315) [![Omega was ready to leave Pabu and embark on her own galactic adventures](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b3/Epilogue-Omega-Hunter.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/290?cb=20240503182315)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b3/Epilogue-Omega-Hunter.png/revision/latest?cb=20240503182315) 

Omega was ready to leave Pabu and embark on her own galactic adventures

 

Omega and her family resided on Pabu. As Omega grew to be an adult, she learned of the [Rebel Alliance's](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic") [fight](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War") against the Empire.[[6]](#cite_note-Cavalry-6) At some point between [2 BBY](/wiki/2_BBY "2 BBY") and [4 ABY](/wiki/4_ABY "4 ABY"),[[68]](#cite_note-RebelDate-68) she decided to answer the Rebellion's calls for new [fighter pilots](/wiki/Rebel_pilot "Rebel pilot"). One night, she prepared to leave Pabu, sneaking down to the cavern where her ship was docked. As she turned on the lamps that illuminated the cavern, she was surprised to see Hunter and Batcher waiting for her. Hunter smiled at her and told her that despite his aging, he could sense that she was trying to sneak off. Omega smiled, saying that he should not be surprised and that she needed to do more to help. Hunter countered that they wanted to keep her safe, and Omega said that they had already done that, reminding him that she was not a kid anymore. Hunter smiled sadly and said that she would always be their kid, and that even if she was ready, he was not. The two embraced, with Omega telling him to keep an eye on Wrecker and Crosshair while she was gone. As Omega also said goodbye to Batcher, Hunter told her that they would always be there for her if she needed them. As she powered up her [ship](/wiki/Omega%27s_ship "Omega's ship"), with Gonky in tow. Preparing for takeoff, Omega saluted to Hunter, who returned the gesture before Omega flew off to join the Rebellion,[[6]](#cite_note-Cavalry-6) which she successfully joined.[[69]](#cite_note-Quiz_227-69)

### Legacy

The [pirate](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate") [Hondo Ohnaka](/wiki/Hondo_Ohnaka "Hondo Ohnaka") recounted Omega's role in the battle between Bane and Shand in his book *[The Secrets of the Bounty Hunters](/wiki/The_Secrets_of_the_Bounty_Hunters "The Secrets of the Bounty Hunters")*, mentioning the young girl whose bounty the two hunters were fighting over.[[70]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Bounty_Hunters-70)

## Personality and traits

:   "*She is my medical assistant. One with a curious mind that causes her to wander.*"
:   ―Nala Se[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1)

 [![Omega was an unmodified clone who had a curious mind.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/OmegaGalaxyOfHeroes.png/revision/latest?cb=20231001095608) [![Omega was an unmodified clone who had a curious mind.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/OmegaGalaxyOfHeroes.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20231001095608)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/OmegaGalaxyOfHeroes.png/revision/latest?cb=20231001095608) 

Omega was an unmodified clone who had a curious mind.

 

Aside from her gender, Omega was an unmodified clone, a pure replica of the original clone template Jango Fett,[[2]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-2) who had spent her entire life on Kamino until she joined the Bad Batch and escaped.[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1) From a young age, the Kaminoans identified Omega as special due to her independent thinking skills and ability to act on them.[[71]](#cite_note-Children-71) Although she was a child, Tech noted that she had a heightened state of awareness.[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1) According to her, she had no behavioral modification biochip.[[26]](#cite_note-Battle_Scars-26) Nala Se was very protective of her, often telling her to stay close by. However, she was not a rule follower and was very curious, investigating the Bad Batch's quarters when they left on a mission.[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1) Before joining the Bad Batch, Omega's constant companion was Nala Se. She had a special relationship with the Kaminoan, who always tried to take care of her.[[53]](#cite_note-Confined-53) Nala Se hired Shand to stop Lama Su from capturing Omega and using her for new cloning technology.[[2]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-2) Even as the Empire held them hostage on Tantiss, Nala Se looked out for Omega, trying to prevent her involvement in the Empire's research[[53]](#cite_note-Confined-53) and helping her escape when she was in trouble.[[54]](#cite_note-Shadows-54)

Omega was compassionate,[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1) boundlessly[[72]](#cite_note-Kamino_Lost_Declassified-72) empathetic,[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1) optimistic, and determinedly positive.[[62]](#cite_note-Harbinger-62) She quickly took a liking to the Bad Batch, looking up to the squad and even copied some of their mannerisms. On Kamino, she repeating Hunter's gestures while sitting next to him[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1) and, onboard the *Marauder*, tried using one of Crosshair's toothpicks like him.[[59]](#cite_note-Infiltration-59) During the Bad Batch's brief imprisonment on Kamino, she consoled Crosshair even though he had made a snide remark about her earlier. As the group tried to make its escape, she saved Wrecker's tooka doll Lula for him amidst the battle. Although she had no combat experience,[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1) Omega was a fast learner, quickly becoming skilled with blasters,[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1)[[54]](#cite_note-Shadows-54) an energy bow, which was her weapon of choice,[[20]](#cite_note-Rampage-20) and hand-to-hand combat.[[53]](#cite_note-Confined-53) Through her time with the Bad Batch, she became a skilled combatant[[73]](#cite_note-Databank-73) and picked up a lot of skills from them. Echo was responsible for helping her practice with her new energy bow.[[20]](#cite_note-Rampage-20) Wrecker instructed her on how to disassemble and defuse explosives.[[27]](#cite_note-Reunion-27) After being instructed by Tech, she became a capable pilot.[[48]](#cite_note-Tipping_Point-48) Tech also made her memorize the Bad Batch's various battle plans, which Omega was able to do.[[54]](#cite_note-Shadows-54) Hunter and Tech both made her study every ship in the Imperial fleet, with Hunter personally quizzing her and Tech making sure she remained diligent with her studies.[[34]](#cite_note-Spoils-34) She was extremely skilled with electronics and technology,[[74]](#cite_note-Comprehensive-74) growing to become even more capable with tools, showcased by her ability to perform maintenance on Gonky.[[32]](#cite_note-War-Mantle-32) Although she had many skills, Omega was also impulsive, rash, and easily frustrated. She was impatient in many occasions, preferring to act instead of wait.[[74]](#cite_note-Comprehensive-74) Coupled with her intelligence,[[73]](#cite_note-Databank-73) resourcefulness,[[28]](#cite_note-Common_Ground-28) determination, bravery, and strategic thinking, she was a formidable member of the squad.[[73]](#cite_note-Databank-73)

 [![Omega was dazzled when experiencing hyperspace for the first time](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a8/OmegaEyesSparkle-Aftermath.png/revision/latest?cb=20220101210901) [![Omega was dazzled when experiencing hyperspace for the first time](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a8/OmegaEyesSparkle-Aftermath.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220101210901)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a8/OmegaEyesSparkle-Aftermath.png/revision/latest?cb=20220101210901) 

Omega was dazzled when experiencing hyperspace for the first time

 

Having spent her entire life in Kamino, Omega had never known anything but the facilities of the Kaminoans and the oceans of Kamino. She was naïve to many of the galaxy's intricacies. She was quick to trust strangers, which got her into some trouble on Pantora when she trusted Fennec Shand,[[19]](#cite_note-Cornered-19) although this friendliness was also helpful during the Bad Batch's mission to Corellia, when Omega quickly became friendly with Trace Martez.[[24]](#cite_note-Decommissioned-24) As the group traveled the galaxy to various planets, she was new to many of the things she saw, from the markets on Ord Mantell[[20]](#cite_note-Rampage-20) and Pantora[[19]](#cite_note-Cornered-19) to even simple things like sunshine and dirt. She was excited by seeing and experiencing new things, becoming fascinated by the soil, plants, and butterflies on Saleucami[[15]](#cite_note-Cut_and_Run-15) and insisting on accompanying Hunter to the [central marketplace](/wiki/Central_marketplace "Central marketplace") when they stopped on Pantora for a resupply so she could see the city.[[19]](#cite_note-Cornered-19) Her strong moral compass allowed her to see through dogma. Omega questioned the ways of the galaxy on multiple occasions.[[71]](#cite_note-Children-71) She was unaware of the phenomenon of slavery until educated on the subject by Tech and Echo and could not believe that it was an accepted practice.[[20]](#cite_note-Rampage-20) She was very skilled with strategy games, helping Cid make money playing dejarik while the other members of the Bad Batch carried out a mission to Raxus.[[28]](#cite_note-Common_Ground-28) While on the run with Crosshair, she was able to hustle over thirty-thousand credits off of various opponents by beating them in balaans.[[55]](#cite_note-Different-55)

As Omega became accustomed to her new life with the Bad Batch, she proved eager to be involved and be a contributing member of the group. She would adopt the action-oriented style of her brothers as well as the clipped and direct ways of speaking that reflected a regimented soldier. As her sense of wonder grew, so did her capabilities,[[75]](#cite_note-Insider-75) and as Omega continued to experience new adventures, she became more and more aware of her potential.[[71]](#cite_note-Children-71) Despite her initial inexperience, her enthusiasm proved useful as she learned to carry out missions with the squad.[[18]](#cite_note-Replacements-18)[[20]](#cite_note-Rampage-20) She felt a sense of duty to help others around them,[[30]](#cite_note-Rescue_on_Ryloth-30) consistently advocating for the squad to intervene when someone needed help.[[74]](#cite_note-Comprehensive-74) When she was left behind when the rest of the Bad Batch traveled to Raxus, she was visibly disappointed to be left out.[[28]](#cite_note-Common_Ground-28) She always spoke up when Hunter wanted to leave her out of missions in an effort to protect her.[[58]](#cite_note-The_Return-58)[[61]](#cite_note-BT-61) Over time, Hunter came to share Omega's readiness to assist those in need.[[74]](#cite_note-Comprehensive-74)

 [![Omega and Wrecker snacked together after every mission](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/OmegaWreckerMantellMix-BS.png/revision/latest?cb=20220109041727) [![Omega and Wrecker snacked together after every mission](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/OmegaWreckerMantellMix-BS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20220109041727)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/OmegaWreckerMantellMix-BS.png/revision/latest?cb=20220109041727) 

Omega and Wrecker snacked together after every mission

 

Omega grew very close to each of her brothers in the squad. Although they were a team of soldiers, they were also Omega's family,[[43]](#cite_note-The_Crossing-43) with the *Marauder* being their home.[[44]](#cite_note-Retrieval-44) Although she once teased Crosshair about being her "little brother," she looked up to all of them.[[58]](#cite_note-The_Return-58) Wrecker's fun-loving personality[[32]](#cite_note-War-Mantle-32) and big heart[[75]](#cite_note-Insider-75) gave her a playful companion. During their time on Ord Mantell, she and Wrecker formed a tradition where they snacked on Mantell Mix after every mission.[[26]](#cite_note-Battle_Scars-26) The two also played board games together during down time.[[32]](#cite_note-War-Mantle-32) She had a strong relationship with Hunter, the first member of the squad to really connect with her,[[18]](#cite_note-Replacements-18) and who acted as a parental guardian towards her.[[27]](#cite_note-Reunion-27) She admired Echo and shared a close bond with him as well.[[74]](#cite_note-Comprehensive-74) Omega very sorrowful when he left to join Rex's operation.[[42]](#cite_note-Truth_and_Consequences-42) She struggled with his departure and was both frustrated and saddened by the changes going on around her, not understanding how the other members of the squad, especially Tech, seemed so unbothered by his absence. She eventually had a conversation with Tech and came to understand that they all felt the weight of their changing circumstances, but processed and expressed that differently.[[43]](#cite_note-The_Crossing-43) When Crosshair returned to the squad following his time with the Imperial Army, Omega was intentional about looking out for him. Although she was grateful to be back with Hunter and Wrecker, she took time to try and help Crosshair readjust. Hunter in particular did not fully trust Crosshair upon his return, but Omega was much more trusting and tried to encourage Crosshair to talk to Hunter so they could become on better terms. When Crosshair and Hunter argued, Omega wanted to step in and help, although Echo told her to stay back and let the two clones work it out.[[58]](#cite_note-The_Return-58) Her bond and loyalty to her brothers only grew over time.[[75]](#cite_note-Insider-75) As much as each member of her squad were her brothers, they were also parental figures to her.[[6]](#cite_note-Cavalry-6) Additionally, she was close with AZI-3, who was a companion for her on Kamino and remained present after leaving the planet.[[74]](#cite_note-Comprehensive-74)

 [![Omega was a friendly and positive person](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/TruthandConsequences-TBB208.png/revision/latest?cb=20230208080658) [![Omega was a friendly and positive person](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/TruthandConsequences-TBB208.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/275?cb=20230208080658)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/TruthandConsequences-TBB208.png/revision/latest?cb=20230208080658) 

Omega was a friendly and positive person

 

During her many adventures with the Bad Batch, Omega enjoyed meeting new people.[[15]](#cite_note-Cut_and_Run-15) Despite Cid's gruffness and eventual betrayal, the Trandoshan had a soft spot for Omega.[[28]](#cite_note-Common_Ground-28) She enjoyed the company of other young people like herself, getting along with Shaeeah and Jek Lawquane,[[15]](#cite_note-Cut_and_Run-15) bonding with Lyana Hazard,[[47]](#cite_note-Pabu-47) and quickly developing a friendship with the young pilot Hera Syndulla, enjoying her appreciation for flying.[[29]](#cite_note-Devil's_Deal-29) She was fascinated by Phee Genoa's stories and tales,[[39]](#cite_note-Entombed-39) being very excited by treasure.[[36]](#cite_note-Ruins-36)[[39]](#cite_note-Entombed-39) Upon meeting Benni Baro, Omega trusted him to help the squad even though he had previously stolen their ship. She was also willing to share [rations](/wiki/Ration_bar "Ration bar") with the boy when she realized that the miners were underfed.[[43]](#cite_note-The_Crossing-43) When Omega was detained in Tantiss for a second time, she was quick to care for the fellow child prisoners, Eva, Jax, Sami, and Bayrn. She was supportive, kind, and helped to inspire hope that they could escape together.[[66]](#cite_note-Breach-66) She also enjoyed being around animals, bonding with a [zardimallo](/wiki/Zardimallo "Zardimallo") [lizard](/wiki/Lizard "Lizard") and naming it Ruby.[[74]](#cite_note-Comprehensive-74) On Pabu, she laughed when a [moon-yo](/wiki/Moonyo "Moonyo") jumped onto her shoulder.[[47]](#cite_note-Pabu-47) In general, Omega understood people[[75]](#cite_note-Insider-75) and saw the best in them. She was quick to trust, forming a rapport with Trace and Rafa Martez almost right away[[24]](#cite_note-Decommissioned-24) and trying to see the good in Emerie Karr even though Karr was helping oversee her imprisonment.[[54]](#cite_note-Shadows-54) She was also very forgiving. Even as Crosshair became their enemy, Omega still treated him as her brother and wanted him to come home.[[33]](#cite_note-Kamino_Lost-33) Although Crosshair saw her optimism as misguided and Royce Hemlock considered her idealism to be a weakness,[[53]](#cite_note-Confined-53) Omega used her compassionate traits to help wherever she could.[[73]](#cite_note-Databank-73)

When Asajj Ventress located Omega on Pabu, she wanted to trust the former Sith apprentice despite her brothers told her about her actions during the Clone Wars. She felt strongly about taking the opportunity to try and discover if she had a high M-count, saying that she had to know what she was. Crosshair thought her trusting Ventress was naive, but Omega convinced the others to give Ventress a chance when she reminded them that people could change, and that she had never given up on Crosshair. She was excited by the notion that she could be a Force-sensitive, but was frustrated by the fact that she did not know how to approach the abstract nature of the tests.[[62]](#cite_note-Harbinger-62)

As Omega reached adulthood, she felt the need to join the Rebel Alliance, wanting to do more to help the galaxy. Although the rest of her squad were done fighting, having survived through the Clone Wars and made peace with leaving the life of a soldier behind, Omega wanted to choose her own cause to fight for. Although Hunter did not want her to leave, he ultimately let her go and allowed her to make her own path through life, giving to Omega something he and the clones of the Grand Army of the Republic had never had during the war and still had trouble with even after the end of the conflict.[[6]](#cite_note-Cavalry-6)

Omega regarded the *Marauder* as home and was upset when Tech insinuated that the ship was merely a mode of transportation after it was stolen on Ipsidon.[[43]](#cite_note-The_Crossing-43) When the Batch prepared to leave Pabu, Omega told Lyana that the Pabu had been the first place that felt like home to her.[[63]](#cite_note-Point_of_No_Return-63)

## Equipment

:   "*I get my own comm device?*"  
    "*Technically, it was Crosshair's, but he doesn't appear to be needing it.*"
:   ―Omega expressed excitement as Tech outfits her with a comlink[[20]](#cite_note-Rampage-20)

 [![Omega practicing with her bow.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/64/OmegaPracticesWithBow-Decommissioned.png/revision/latest?cb=20220108050515) [![Omega practicing with her bow.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/64/OmegaPracticesWithBow-Decommissioned.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20220108050515)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/64/OmegaPracticesWithBow-Decommissioned.png/revision/latest?cb=20220108050515) 

Omega practicing with her bow.

 

During her time on Kamino, Omega wore a white tunic with red-and-blue sleeves, black pants, and black [boots](/wiki/Boot "Boot"). She had a Kaminoan-style forehead pendant which she wore in her hair,[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1) although she removed it and altered her hairstyle after escaping Saleucami.[[15]](#cite_note-Cut_and_Run-15) Her overall outfit reflected that of Nala Se. During the mission to Ord Mantell, Tech provided her with a [wrist-mounted communicator](/wiki/Wrist_comm "Wrist comm"), which had formerly been Crosshair's. When the wrist comm was destroyed by Cad Bane on Bora Vio[[2]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-2) she was provided with a standard [comlink](/wiki/Comlink "Comlink").[[30]](#cite_note-Rescue_on_Ryloth-30) On the same mission she had been given the wrist comm, she acquired a retractable Zygerrian energy bow[[20]](#cite_note-Rampage-20) that she went on to use in combat.[[76]](#cite_note-Bad_Batch_Trailer-76) However, she was quite ineffective using the weapon at first due to not being practiced or strong enough to shoot straight.[[24]](#cite_note-Decommissioned-24) In time, she became skilled with the weapon.[[50]](#cite_note-Plan_99-50) Echo later gifted her a modified [energy crossbow](/wiki/Energy_crossbow "Energy crossbow") on Teth, which Omega was thankful to receive.[[59]](#cite_note-Infiltration-59)

 [![Omega's regular outfit during her adventures](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Omega-TBBs2.png/revision/latest?cb=20230210012127) [![Omega's regular outfit during her adventures](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Omega-TBBs2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230210012127)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Omega-TBBs2.png/revision/latest?cb=20230210012127) 

Omega's regular outfit during her adventures

 

Omega would eventually leave behind the simple tunic of Kamino and wear a red shirt, a blue jacket, a brown bandolier and belt, gray pants, and brown boots. During missions, she frequently wore a[[34]](#cite_note-Spoils-34) speeder courier helmet[[9]](#cite_note-Dawn_Guide-9) and sometimes carried a backpack.[[34]](#cite_note-Spoils-34) As Omega's hair grew out, she wore a small ponytail.[[53]](#cite_note-Confined-53) After being rescued from Tantiss Base and returning to Pabu, Omega was outfitted with a pale green shirt, a knit green sweater vest, and a simple necklace.[[58]](#cite_note-The_Return-58) She later wore a white shirt with a brown jacket.[[61]](#cite_note-BT-61) As an adult, Omega had a jacket that was orange and tan denim fabric with slightly reflective yellow shoulders. The jacket included a patch on the right shoulder that depicting the black and red Bad Batch emblem. Her thin blue pants were synthetic spacesuit material. She had black boots and also wore gloves.[[77]](#cite_note-Older_Omega-77) Finally, Omega carried a brown bag,[[6]](#cite_note-Cavalry-6) had an orange pendant around her neck, and a red bandana in her hair.[[77]](#cite_note-Older_Omega-77)

During her time on Pantora, Omega ended up taking a clone trooper doll without paying for it.[[19]](#cite_note-Cornered-19) She considered the toy trooper to be a female like herself, painting its armor black to make the doll a member of the Bad Batch.[[20]](#cite_note-Rampage-20) For Omega, the doll was not only one of her only playthings and a comfort to her when she was scared, but a connection to her past life on Kamino as well as her new life with the Bad Batch.[[78]](#cite_note-Doll_DB-78) She also co-owned Wrecker's [tooka doll](/wiki/Tooka_doll "Tooka doll"), [Lula](/wiki/Lula "Lula"),[[18]](#cite_note-Replacements-18) sleeping with it on occasion.[[58]](#cite_note-The_Return-58)

By the time she left Pabu to join the Rebellion, Omega had her own [ship](/wiki/Omega%27s_ship "Omega's ship"), which included several mementos of her squad aboard. Tech's goggles sat in the cockpit, while Lula sat in a seat located in the ship's cabin.[[6]](#cite_note-Cavalry-6)

## Behind the scenes

### Development and early seasons

:   "*The interesting challenge was: How do you challenge a super soldier? And what can you throw at them that's something that they're not equipped to deal with? That's how the idea of Omega came to be. Soldiers can figure things out, but what they've never had to deal with is a young kid. And that completely changes how they relate to one another and changes their perspective on the galaxy... You drop them into a Separatist battlefront and they're going to be fine no matter what. But having to be guardians and be responsible for the upbringing and rearing of a child is something totally different.*"
:   ―Jennifer Corbett, *The Bad Batch* head writer[[79]](#cite_note-Corbett_Interview-79)

Omega was created for the [2021](/wiki/2021 "2021") [Disney+](/wiki/Disney%2B "Disney+") series *[Star Wars: The Bad Batch](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Bad_Batch "Star Wars: The Bad Batch")*. She was first revealed on [March 30](/wiki/March_30 "March 30") of that year in a trailer for the show which gave the character's name in the closed captioning.[[76]](#cite_note-Bad_Batch_Trailer-76) Her first appearance was in the series premiere, "[Aftermath](/wiki/Aftermath_(episode) "Aftermath (episode)")." She is voiced by [Michelle Ang](/wiki/Michelle_Ang "Michelle Ang"),[[1]](#cite_note-Aftermath-1) who was delighted to be a part of the Star Wars universe. She had originally auditioned for a role in the [2017](/wiki/2017 "2017") film [*Star Wars:* Episode VIII *The Last Jedi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VIII_The_Last_Jedi "Star Wars: Episode VIII The Last Jedi"), the second installment of the *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* [sequel trilogy](/wiki/Sequel_trilogy "Sequel trilogy"). and was heartbroken when she did not get the part. Admittedly, she did not realize she was auditioning for a *Star Wars* project when she tried out, but was delighted when she learned she was finally entering the *Star Wars* universe, and felt the satisfaction of having come full circle. When recording her lines, Ang did much of the work from her own home as opposed to being in the recording studio, noting that it was much more comfortable that way and that it allowed her to be more physical in her performance.[[80]](#cite_note-Meet_Omega-80) For the final recording session, Ang joined her co-star [Dee Bradley Baker](/wiki/Dee_Bradley_Baker "Dee Bradley Baker") in the studio at Lucasfilm headquarters. Ang felt lucky to be working alongside Baker, saying she felt that they both agreed on morality being important to their characters and to the show overall. Baker agreed, asserting Omega was the moral compass and the character that powered the story.[[81]](#cite_note-Finale_Interview-81)

 [![Michelle Ang, who voices Omega.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/MichelleAng.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210504222148) [![Michelle Ang, who voices Omega.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/MichelleAng.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20210504222148)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/MichelleAng.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210504222148) 

Michelle Ang, who voices Omega.

 

Throughout the series, Ang's approach to Omega evolved. In later seasons, Ang did not pitch her voice up as much to reflect Omega's growing maturity, which she felt was also complemented by thoughtfulness from the writers when constructing her dialogue.[[82]](#cite_note-Soldier_and_Survivor-82) In season one, she was not shy about suggesting changes to the script during script-readings, wanting to emphasize Omega's child-like perspective whenever possible. Many conversations were had about how to balance Omega's cheeky or sassy sides with her "grown-upness."[[80]](#cite_note-Meet_Omega-80) In season two, Ang and director [Brad Rau](/wiki/Brad_Rau "Brad Rau") described the evolution of Omega's personality as growing into "Good Soldier Omega," which entailed more clipped, direct ways of speaking and less of the excessive expressiveness. Ang also noted that as much as she drew on her own life experiences in the recording booth, her son was also a big inspiration to her portrayal of Omega's youthful confidence and newfound audaciousness.[[82]](#cite_note-Soldier_and_Survivor-82) Although she did not feel like her son was old enough to enjoy or appreciate the show in the beginning, when he was only four years old,[[80]](#cite_note-Meet_Omega-80) as he grew, they began to watch the episodes together each week.[[82]](#cite_note-Soldier_and_Survivor-82)

Rau acknowledged Omega's relationship with the other members of the Bad Batch as being both a sibling bond[[83]](#cite_note-Look_Back-83) as well as a parental bond, thinking of the other clones as both Omega's brothers in one sense and her dads in another.[[84]](#cite_note-Empire_is_Everywhere-84) Baker also acknowledged this complexity in their relationship.[[85]](#cite_note-Buckle_Up-85) The creators took care to spend time on Omega's relationship with each of her brothers individually. While the show's [first season](/wiki/The_Bad_Batch_Season_1 "The Bad Batch Season 1") spent more time on Omega's connection with Hunter and Wrecker, the [second season](/wiki/The_Bad_Batch_Season_2 "The Bad Batch Season 2") delved more into Omega's relationships with Echo and Tech.[[84]](#cite_note-Empire_is_Everywhere-84) Finally, the [third season](/wiki/The_Bad_Batch_Season_3 "The Bad Batch Season 3") showcased the dynamic between Omega and Crosshair.[[83]](#cite_note-Look_Back-83)

The music that became [Omega's Theme](/wiki/Omega%27s_Theme "Omega's Theme") was originally written by [Sean Kiner](/wiki/Sean_Kiner "Sean Kiner"), who collaborated with [Kevin](/wiki/Kevin_Kiner "Kevin Kiner") and [Deana Kiner](/wiki/Deana_Kiner "Deana Kiner") on the show's score. Kiner noted that he was inspired by the birth of his daughter, a moment that he drew from to create the sense of hope and optimism in the theme. The track's original B section eventually became the main A section.[[86]](#cite_note-Kiners-86)

Omega's introduction to the [2015](/wiki/2015 "2015") [EA Capital Games](/wiki/EA_Capital_Games "EA Capital Games") [video game](/wiki/Star_Wars_video_games "Star Wars video games") *[Star Wars: Galaxy of Heroes](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galaxy_of_Heroes "Star Wars: Galaxy of Heroes")*[[87]](#cite_note-SWGOH-87) was teased in a forum post on [July 13](/wiki/July_13 "July 13"), 2021, following the release of the show's first season.[[88]](#cite_note-Forum_Post-88) Later, another version of the character inspired by the latter two seasons of *The Bad Batch*, Omega (Fugitive), was revealed on [January 15](/wiki/January_15 "January 15"), [2025](/wiki/2025 "2025").[[89]](#cite_note-Kit_Reveal-89)

### Season three finale

:   "*We weren't set on exactly how it was going to end. There were sort of some exploration, but as an actor, an emotional moment was the ending we landed on. It was like the culmination of my journey as a performer and Omega's journey as a character all consolidated into, two lines.*"
:   ―Michelle Ang[[90]](#cite_note-Omega_Season_3-90)

Due to her history with the show and her character, it was difficult for Ang to even open the script for the series finale. Ang promised the series finale would be very sentimental[[90]](#cite_note-Omega_Season_3-90) and satisfying.[[91]](#cite_note-Behind_the_Geeks-91) She further promised that Omega's final moments on screen had a great gravity to them, thereby culminating "everything" at play in a bittersweet ending. In one interview, she also revealed Omega originally had a different ending, which would have opened the door for her to have a very important future in the overall *Star Wars* galaxy, but it was changed "from there" into the bittersweet ending.[[90]](#cite_note-Omega_Season_3-90) All the same, she expressed in another interview her hopes that Omega's story would have larger ramifications on the *Star Wars* galaxy and even open a door for her to appear in a live action production, which was where she mainly did acting work.[[91]](#cite_note-Behind_the_Geeks-91)

 [![The final Bad Batch character poster, released the same day as the series finale](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/BadBatchFamily-CharPoster-TBBS3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240501164652) [![The final Bad Batch character poster, released the same day as the series finale](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/BadBatchFamily-CharPoster-TBBS3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20240501164652)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/BadBatchFamily-CharPoster-TBBS3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240501164652) 

The final Bad Batch character poster, released the same day as the series finale

 

Rau noted that Omega's role in the series finale was comparable to Hunter's role in the Bad Batch—explaining that "Hunter-Omega" was forced to lead, be calm, and take charge in order to help the other imprisoned children. Rau felt it was a full-circle moment for the character and was impressed by Ang's ability to portray Omega in these scenes. The show's co-creator and head writer [Jennifer Corbett](/wiki/Jennifer_Corbett "Jennifer Corbett") felt that it was a good parallel to the [first episode](/wiki/Aftermath_(episode) "Aftermath (episode)") of the show, where the Bad Batch had to rescue Omega themselves. In this episode, Omega, using all her training, was able to break out and help the other children escape without needing help from her squad.[[83]](#cite_note-Look_Back-83)

While the epilogue scene was always in the minds of the show's creators, the actual events of the scene were always in flux. Corbett noted discussions about the epilogue happened as early as Season 1, but the final version of the scene was not nailed down until Season 3. Each member of the team felt they had a certain connection to the scene, with Corbett noting how personal it felt as a parallel to her own choice to join the military and Rau comparing it to the bittersweet emotions of sending two kids off to college.[[83]](#cite_note-Look_Back-83) Ang also felt that Omega's journey was a reflection of her own personal journey. She felt it was important for Omega to emerge from the story as resilient and ready to start a new chapter, choosing a life that she felt compelled to live. Ang ultimately used something closer to her normal voice for the epilogue scene.[[81]](#cite_note-Finale_Interview-81)

### Contradictions

[![StarWarsKids](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://www.youtube.com/c/StarWarsKids) [8 of the Best Buddies in Star Wars | Star Wars: List It!](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=a8pt85FAJuc) on the official [*Star Wars* Kids](/wiki/StarWarsKids.com "StarWarsKids.com") [YouTube channel](https://www.youtube.com/c/StarWarsKids) ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20220425072830/https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=a8pt85FAJuc)) states that Omega is around the same age as [Shaeeah](/wiki/Shaeeah_Lawquane "Shaeeah Lawquane") and [Jek Lawquane](/wiki/Jek_Lawquane "Jek Lawquane"). [![StarWars.com](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") [*The Clone Wars* Episode Guide: The Deserter](https://web.archive.org/web/20110629042704/https://www.starwars.com/theclonewars/guide/episode210.html) on [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") ([original site](https://www.starwars.com/theclonewars/guide/episode210.html) is defunct) states that Jek was four and Shaeeah was five [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") old during the events of "[The Deserter](/wiki/The_Deserter "The Deserter")." *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates the events of "[The Deserter](/wiki/The_Deserter "The Deserter")" to [21 BBY](/wiki/21_BBY "21 BBY"). However, as the [2002](/wiki/2002 "2002") film [*Star Wars*: Episode II *Attack of the Clones*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones "Star Wars: Episode II Attack of the Clones"), the second installment of the *Star Wars* [prequel trilogy](/wiki/Prequel_trilogy "Prequel trilogy"), establishes that the [clones](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") of [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett") required a [decade](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade") of growth to reach adulthood, and *Star Wars: The Bad Batch* portrays Omega as being older than the other members of [Clone Force 99](/wiki/Clone_Force_99 "Clone Force 99"), who were adults by [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"), this seems to be in conflict with previous sources. Moreover, the statement regarding Omega's age may not have been intended literally, and the *[Star Wars: List It!](/wiki/Star_Wars:_List_It! "Star Wars: List It!")* series of videos has since been removed from [StarWarsKids.com](/wiki/StarWarsKids.com "StarWarsKids.com"). Therefore, this article does not assume the statement to establish an exact [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") of Omega's birth.

Encyclopedia](/wiki/Star_Wars_Encyclopedia_(series) "Star Wars Encyclopedia (series)")* 4. [↑](#cite_ref-HeightDate_4-0) Per the reasoning [here](/wiki/Template:TBBS2Date "Template:TBBS2Date"), [Season 2](/wiki/The_Bad_Batch_Season_2 "The Bad Batch Season 2") of *[Star Wars: The Bad Batch](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Bad_Batch "Star Wars: The Bad Batch")* takes place around [18 BBY](/wiki/18_BBY "18 BBY"). The tally marks made by **Omega** in [*The Bad Batch* Season 3's](/wiki/The_Bad_Batch_Season_3 "The Bad Batch Season 3") first episode, "[Confined](/wiki/Confined "Confined")," indicate the episode must take place at least twenty-one [standard days](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day") following her capture as depicted in the Season 2 episode "[Plan 99](/wiki/Plan_99_(episode) "Plan 99 (episode)")." According to [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") ["Confined" Trivia Guide | Star Wars The Bad Batch](https://www.starwars.com/confined-trivia-gallery-star-wars-the-bad-batch) on [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20240229062058/https://www.starwars.com/confined-trivia-gallery-star-wars-the-bad-batch)), Omega spends about 164 further days in captivity by the end of "Confined." As such, the events of Season 3 must begin around 18 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system"). 5. [↑](#cite_ref-Date_40-0) Per the reasoning [here](/wiki/Template:TruthAndConsequencesDate "Template:TruthAndConsequencesDate"), the seventh and eighth episodes of [*The Bad Batch* Season 2](/wiki/The_Bad_Batch_Season_2 "The Bad Batch Season 2"), "[The Clone Conspiracy](/wiki/The_Clone_Conspiracy "The Clone Conspiracy")" and "[Truth and Consequences](/wiki/Truth_and_Consequences "Truth and Consequences")," can be placed in [18 BBY](/wiki/18_BBY "18 BBY"). Therefore, all Season 2 episodes proceeding "The Clone Conspiracy" occur between [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"), which features the end of [*The Bad Batch* Season 1](/wiki/The_Bad_Batch_Season_1 "The Bad Batch Season 1") according to *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")*, and 18 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system"). The [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"), the [formation](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") of which *Star Wars: Timelines* dates to 19 BBY, sent [Mayday's squad](/wiki/Mayday%27s_squad "Mayday's squad") to [Barton IV](/wiki/Barton_IV "Barton IV") over a [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") prior to the events of the twelfth episode, "[The Outpost](/wiki/The_Outpost "The Outpost")." As it occurs over a year into the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era") and is set shortly after the events of "Truth and Consequences," the events of "The Outpost" occur around 18 BBY. Following that logic, the ninth through eleventh episodes ("[The Crossing](/wiki/The_Crossing "The Crossing")" through "[Metamorphosis](/wiki/Metamorphosis_(episode) "Metamorphosis (episode)")") are also set around 18 BBY because they occur between the events of "Truth and Consequences" and "The Outpost." Finally, all season 2 episodes set after "The Outpost" occur shortly after its events, thereby placing those episodes around 18 BBY as well. 41. ↑ [41.0](#cite_ref-Tribe_41-0) [↑](#cite_ref-RebelDate_68-0) *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates the [Declaration of the Rebel Alliance](/wiki/Declaration_of_the_Rebel_Alliance "Declaration of the Rebel Alliance") to [2 BBY](/wiki/2_BBY "2 BBY"). *Timelines* also dates the Rebel Alliance's reorganization into the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic") to [4 ABY](/wiki/4_ABY "4 ABY"). Therefore, the epilogue of "The Cavalry Has Arrived" must take place between 2 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system") and 4 ABY. 69.
